Domestic News Two

Quiet War Situation in Guangxi Province 62

▲ Guangdong Army Sends Troops to Suppress Bandits on the Southern Border

Guangzhou Correspondence: The war in Guangxi has been quiet for a long time. When Chen Jitang returned to Guangdong a few days ago, it was claimed externally that Yu Hanmou's division had occupied Binyang. According to a recent investigation, Yu's division only approached Binyang on that day. Because the enemy army was still stationed with heavy troops in Qianjiang, he had to proceed cautiously. In recent days, he has still been making arrangements, and the war situation at the front has been quite quiet. According to a recent report from Chen Hanguang, the head of the Guard Regiment stationed in Guixian, the actual situation is as follows: 1. Yu Hanmou, the commander of the column, has now decided to attack Binyang, cutting off the connection between the Yong and Liu rebel armies in order to divide the troops and suppress them. He has recently ordered the 59th Division and the Huang Brigade's Fan Regiment to advance fiercely towards Binyang. This regiment (i.e., the Guard Regiment) was ordered by Commander Yu to travel by boat from Da Huangjiang to Guixian, and then advance by land to launch a major offensive against the enemy. 2. It is reported that the rebel army has gathered seven or eight thousand men near Binyang to fight a decisive battle with us. The rebel army lacks food and ammunition, and its morale is disintegrating. If our army arrives, we can annihilate them. The Binyang battle should break out during the daytime. Our army has been very busy preparing for military affairs in recent days. 3. The rebel army has now tilted the remaining enemies from Liu and Yong in an attempt to make a final struggle with our army. They are bound to fail. If this battle is fought, the military situation in Guangxi can be resolved, etc. As for the enemy army, the majority are still concentrated in Liuzhou. Recently, due to supply difficulties, most of the soldiers are short of food, and the military equipment cannot be replenished. It is reported that the Guangxi army, Huang Shaoxiong, recently purchased a batch of bullets from a certain place and remitted 300,000 yuan in cash, which will be transported from Chikan in Guangzhou Bay to Luchuan on the Guangxi border to supply a certain Lu on the Guangdong-Guangxi border, allowing him to harass the Guangdong border. This matter was discovered by Li Jiezhi, the commander of the Second Independent Regiment stationed in the army. He telegraphed the Eighth Route Army Headquarters yesterday, and the Headquarters telegraphed Li to quickly send troops to distribute in Lianjiang, Huazhou, Maoming, and Xinyi to strictly guard against disasters. Therefore, the southern road of Guangdong Province has recently been prepared for bandit defense. In order to report on the defense of the area, Chen Zhangfu, the commander of the Southern Route Garrison, took the Beihai Wheel at the end of last month and arrived in the province on the 1st to report everything to Chen Jitang. Chen will return to defense about a week later. Recently, in order to prevent border bandits from causing trouble, the military authorities of the province added Zhong Fangjun's entire First Independent Regiment to Zhaoqing to assist the Third Battalion of the regiment, which was previously suppressing bandits in the Yunfu area. Moreover, Zhaoqing is adjacent to the southern road, and the terrain is important, so more capable troops must be sent to quickly quell the banditry in the area to reassure travelers. After receiving the order, the commander of the regiment led the First and Second Battalions on the 2nd, taking more than ten civilian ships to various places in Zhaoqing to defend against and suppress bandits. (August 3rd)

After Fuzhou's Special Martial Law 63

▲ More Than 30 Checkpoints Established

Fuzhou dispatch: In recent days, the Martial Law Headquarters has received repeated intelligence reports that reactionary elements are lurking in the city, plotting unrest. After convening a joint military and police conference, it was decided to implement special martial law starting on the 1st. Traffic would be cut off after 10 PM every day. Except for public officials with passwords who are allowed to pass, no one else would be allowed to pass. All theaters are allowed to perform daytime shows but prohibited from performing nighttime shows. More than 30 checkpoints were established at key strategic locations on the city walls. The temporary budget for each location is set at ten yuan. Specifically, the area of the First Precinct of the City Wall, West Gate Street, is to be the responsibility of the 336th Regiment. The area in front of Jingloumen Gongyuan is to be the responsibility of the special service company of the 168th Brigade. The North Gate and Yingwei are to be the responsibility of the 2nd Company of the 332nd Regiment. The Second Precinct, East Gate Tangmen, is to be the responsibility of the 336th Regiment. The Water Gate and Nanmendou are to be the responsibility of the 56th Division Cavalry Company. Qifan Kou is to be the responsibility of the 56th Division Special Service Battalion. Huaidefang Jindouqiao Shuangpaoqiao Maotoushan are to be the responsibility of the 332nd Regiment. Gaojieli Mingluntang is to be the responsibility of the 332nd Regiment. The Third Precinct, Xiaoqiao Youxiang Xiayangtoukou Sanbao Zhongjie Makoujie Baimaqiao, is to be the responsibility of the 2nd Regiment of the 1st Marine Brigade. The Fourth Precinct, Daqiaotou Zhongdunkou Pingli Nan Gongyuan Shuibu Zhuangyuanjing, is to be the responsibility of the 336th Regiment. The Fifth Precinct, Sanyikou Daling Xi Xiangtoujie Duihu Shangdujie Maiyunding Shipu, is to be the responsibility of the 2nd Regiment of the 2nd Brigade. The simplified rules for the joint military and police temporary checkpoints consist of six articles. Articles 1 (Purpose), 5 (Rewards and Punishments), and 6 (Supplementary Provisions) are omitted. Article 3 (Establishment Location and Military-Police Assignment) is as described above. Articles 2 and 4 are listed below. Article 2, Organization and System: 1. Each location is designated as a Joint Military and Police Temporary Checkpoint at a certain location in Fuzhou City. 2. Each checkpoint is to have one Director, to be held by the military officer stationed at that location. 3. Each checkpoint is jointly organized by military and police, under the command of the Director, specifically responsible for checkpoint duties. 4. Each checkpoint, regardless of troop strength, should have a platoon leader permanently stationed at the location, to be able to handle matters appropriately in case of emergency, to ensure caution. 5. In addition to being supervised by their respective direct military and police superiors, the military and police at each checkpoint are also under the command of Headquarters. Article 4, Checkpoint Rules: 1. Check suspicious pedestrians for the presence of concealed military weapons. 2. Check people's transported boxes, crates, and miscellaneous items for the presence of concealed military weapons. 3. Anyone found to be secretly carrying various military weapons should be immediately detained along with the contraband and sent to Headquarters for verification and handling, while also reporting to their direct superior. However, from the time of discovery, reports and transfers should be made separately within one hour, and they should not be detained in the station for long or handled privately, and especially not allow the principal to escape. If there is concern about escape during transfer, Headquarters may be requested to send troops to escort them. 4. Anyone found to be in possession of any prohibited items (such as white pills and opium) should also be detained along with the perpetrator and handed over to the relevant police station for transfer to the Public Security Bureau for legal processing. At the same time, the type and quantity of the contraband and the names and number of perpetrators should be reported separately to Headquarters and their direct superiors for record keeping. The resulting bonus should be fairly distributed by Headquarters in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau. 5. Checkpoints must not arbitrarily delay matters or deliberately create difficulties, and should release people as soon as they are checked. 6. All checkpoints must adopt an extremely peaceful attitude and must not be rude or impolite. If someone refuses to be checked, they must be kindly persuaded. If they genuinely resist being checked, they may be detained and handed over to Headquarters for verification. 7. Except for cases of secretly carrying military weapons and contraband where both people and goods are detained, no other people's property may be taken without permission. 8. Checkpoint hours: apply at any time, day or night, whenever there are pedestrians on the road. 9. Each checkpoint should rotate in shifts according to the number of military and police personnel, performing checkpoint duties, and must always be at a suitable location on the road, checking at any time. The rotation and distribution methods are to be determined by the Director. 10. Regarding the checking of suspicious women, each relevant police station should find ways to handle it nearby. 11. Military and police at checkpoints, regarding military discipline and conduct, in addition to being supervised and commanded by the Director, their direct superiors must also bear the responsibility of supervision and command. (September 2nd)

Communist Bandits Near Changsha Have Been Repelled 64

Hankou dispatch: Previously, the communist bandits Peng Dehuai, Huang Gonglue, Kong Hechong, etc., in Changsha, Pingjiang, Liuyang, and other places in Hunan Province, were head-on attacked severely by He Jian's troops of the Fourth Route Army and the Gong and Luo Divisions, suffering great losses and fleeing to the border of Jiangxi. They regrouped with the remnants and were again defeated by the Jiangxi army, fleeing to the Tonggu and Xiushui areas on the Jiangxi border to join up with Zhu De and Mao Zedong's troops. Recently, they gathered again about 30,000 to 40,000 people and invaded Pingliu at the end of last month. At the beginning of this month, Peng Dehuai again led the 5th and 6th Armies through Pingliu to Huanghuashi near Changsha. Zhu and Mao led the 11th and 12th Armies, and Huang Gonglue and Lin Biao led the 4th and 6th Armies (a communist army usually has 5,000 to 6,000 men, but sometimes as few as 1,000 to 2,000 men) from the Zhuzhou area, through Pujishi and Zhentoushi to Guandaopu, attempting to re-invade Changsha, making a desperate gamble. He Jian, Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army, believing that the communist army was coming fiercely, decided to shorten the battle line, lure them deep, and then attack again. The Hankou Xingying [Field Headquarters], for the sake of overall suppression, also transferred the New 5th Division under Gong Bingfan, the New 22nd Division under Luo Lin, the 3rd Teaching Division under Qian Dajun, and the New 3rd Division under Li Yunlong, to advance towards Tongcheng, Pingjiang, Liuyang, Changsha, and other places from various directions. It also dispatched naval vessels such as the Xianning and Yongsheng to sail to the Changsha River surface, as well as stationed Hankou's Curtiss Hawk and other fighter planes, and Xiangjiang seaplanes and other aircraft, to fly to assist in the battle, conduct ground reconnaissance and bombing. It also ordered the Hunan Provincial Qingxiang [Purge Countryside] Command to guide farmers in various districts to organize Farmers' Communist Elimination Volunteer Teams to assist the army and jointly defend against the bandits, so as to prevent the bandits from fleeing to various townships and disturbing the people. After receiving the order from the Hankou Xingying, He Jian planned everything, and at the beginning of this month, he had completed the deployment of all troops and constructed defensive fortresses in the suburbs, arranging three layers of electrified wire, with extremely solid works. On the 1st and 2nd of this month, there were small contacts in the suburbs of Changsha from time to time, but the gains and losses were very small and unimportant. Since the 3rd, He Jian believed that the time was ripe and ordered Luo Lin's division on the left wing to attack from Laodaoh River towards Baimaopu, Tao Guang's division to attack from Houzishi on the right wing, and Chen Guangzhong's brigade to cross the river from Datopu to encircle and attack the bandits from the side and rear. One side ordered the Xianning and Yongsheng ships patrolling the river surface to continuously bombard the communist army on the right bank from the upper reaches of Houzishi. Curtiss Hawk and other fighter planes and Xiangjiang seaplanes flew over the enemy's positions from time to time, bombing important parts of the enemy and lowering to a thousand feet to strafe with machine guns. After two days of fierce fighting, the communist army under Kong Hechong on the right wing was attacked by Luo's division, and countless were killed or wounded, and hundreds of guns were captured. At 1:00 PM on the 3rd, Luo's division occupied Baimaopu Zhanggongling, and the bandits collapsed in a southeasterly direction. The communist bandits under Peng Dehuai on the left route were attacked by Tao's division and also collapsed in disorder. A part of them fled to Changle, which was intercepted and attacked by the Li Tuan stationed in Yuezhou, advancing to Miluo. According to aircraft reports, on the 4th, all armies launched an attack on all fronts, and the left, right, and center routes all achieved victories, killing countless bandits. By 5:00 PM, the bandit forces were unable to hold out, and the bandits in Huangwangling and Lannichong retreated southeast towards Dongjingpu, while the bandits in Letang and Dongshan retreated to the vicinity of Houjiachong and Baizhutang, in an extremely embarrassed state. Aircraft carried eight heavy bombs and dropped them along the retreat route of the communist army, killing a total of hundreds of bandits. The Xiangjiang seaplane dropped two 60-pound bombs in a communist bandit den at the Southern Route Cotton Industry Testing Ground on the 3rd. At that time, more than a thousand communist bandits had gathered in the field, and hundreds were also killed. Currently, all armies are pursuing and advancing, encircling and suppressing them in separate directions. It is rumored that Peng and Huang suffered heavy losses and planned to flee to Chaling and the Lianhua area on the border of Hunan, returning to their old nest in Jinggang to prolong their existence. The military authorities are currently pursuing and suppressing them. (September 5th)

Jiangxi Provincial Government Reports on the Situation of Communist Bandits 65

Nanchang dispatch: Communist bandits in Jiangxi Province are the most rampant. The Provincial Government yesterday released a report on the recent situation of communist bandits and the general situation of suppression. The original text is as follows:

▲ Situation of Communist Bandits (1) Zhu Mao in Western Jiangxi: After Zhu Mao's bandit troops failed to invade the Niuhang Railway Station from Gaoan and Fengxin last month, they fled from Shanggao and Yifeng to Wanzai, reorganized the sentinel teams into pseudo-peasant self-defense forces, and held a meeting in Daqiao on July 16th, deciding to jointly disrupt Hunan and Hubei with the pseudo 1st and 2nd Army Corps. After the meeting, they fled towards Daqiao Zhutan. On the 17th, there were no traces of bandits in Wanzai City. They then fled from Daqiao to Tanbu Huangmao Pingjiang, forming a line with the Peng bandits in Pingjiang, and invaded Changsha. (2) Fang Zhimin in Eastern Jiangxi: 1. Fang's bandits attacked and captured Yujiang on August 10th, massacring more than 500 people, with huge property losses. 2. Hu Zhaoxiang and other reactionaries in Yiyang colluded with the county police team to rebel, killing county party committee members Fang Du, Fang Keqiang, Fan Wenying, Xie Zechun, etc. Fang's bandits took advantage of the chaos and captured the city on August 5th, with hundreds of civilians killed. 3. The city walls of Leping had been dismantled long ago, making defense difficult. The provincial and county police teams stationed there guarded different areas. Fang's bandits attacked with all their forces on August 19th. The police team fought unfavorably, and the city fell the next day. 4. Poyang is an important town in northern Jiangxi. The county police team has 500 guns, and the county magistrate is the commander of the first district, so it was believed that it could be secured without worry. Unexpectedly, at dawn on August 27th, it was suddenly breached by Fang's bandits. According to a section member of the provincial government who escaped from the county, the county police team was stationed outside the city, leading to the bandits taking advantage of the situation. (3) Bandits in various counties are stirring up trouble: 1. The 2nd and 3rd Red bandit corps under Ke Wudong and Li Shaojiu, with 400 to 500 guns and 2,000 to 3,000 men, captured Xiajiang on August 21st. 2. Bandits in Tonggu Paibu and Pingtan colluded with more than 1,000 bandits who had dispersed from Zhu Mao in Yifeng, with 400 guns, killing everywhere. Approaching the county seat, most of the ripe rice in the countryside was harvested by them. 3. About 400 to 500 hooligans and local bullies in Ningdu held a meeting in Dongcaojiang near the county, organizing a pseudo-Soviet government. 4. The 20th Red Army under Li Yunxiu led more than 3,000 men, with about 800 guns, crossed the river at dawn attempting to attack Ji'an, but were defeated by the New 13th Division. 5. The 22nd Red Army, with about 1,000 men and hundreds of guns, approached the edge of Ganxian city, but were forced to flee towards Mojiashan by Ma's brigade of the 12th Division. 6. In Xiushui, there is a bandit leader Fang Guomin claiming to be the commander of the pseudo Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi Border Defense Team, with about 400 guns, entrenched in Mashi, 60 li from the city. The county militia has gathered more than 10,000 people, blocking the key points in separate directions. 7. The bandit leader Huang Jiafa, claiming to be the commander-in-chief of the 14th Red Army, with about hundreds of men and dozens of guns, colluded with local bullies and hooligans in Gaoan Fenghuangjing, wantonly harassing. It is said that the bandits opposed Zhu Mao's unfair distribution of spoils and withdrew on their own, setting up their own banner. 8. The bandits in Yifeng Tianbao, a part of them have already fled with Zhu Mao, and another part is still haunting the area. The county is currently planning to encircle and suppress them. 9. In Nanfeng, there are more than a hundred bandits, with forty guns, gathering people in Poyangpu to establish a farmers' association. From the above, except for Zhu Mao and Fang Zhimin, the rest are mobs and cannot withstand a single blow. If the local self-defense capabilities are strengthened day by day, these jumping clowns will not be able to cause trouble.

▲ General Situation of Suppression (1) Commander-in-Chief Chiang ordered all 50 divisions to return to Jiangxi to suppress the bandits. Yue's brigade arrived in Jiujiang on August 31st and is currently stationed in the Nansun Road area. It is reported that Cheng and Luo's brigades are being transferred. (2) The Capital Special Service 3rd Regiment opened to Xun for joint defense. Jiujiang was originally defended by the Capital Special Service 2nd Regiment. To strengthen the force, the National Government sent the 3rd Regiment under Zhang Yuannan to open to Xun, which arrived on the 28th. The military appearance is very orderly, and the defense of Xun is more solid. (3) Curtiss Hawk fighter planes arrived in the province. The Central Government had previously sent the Moth aircraft to Jiangxi to assist in suppressing the communist bandits. Chairman Lu believed that the aircraft missions were numerous during the bandit suppression period, and specially requested the Central Government to send another Curtiss Hawk fighter plane to Jiangxi. The aircraft has flown from Beijing to the province and has been conducting reconnaissance of bandit activity and bombing bandit nests for days, with significant results. (4) Guangdong and Zhejiang provinces sent troops to Jiangxi to assist in suppressing the bandits. Guangdong Chairman Chen has agreed to Chairman Lu's request to transfer a regiment to be stationed in Ganxian. The provincial government telegraphed the county magistrate Wang of the county to represent the welcome. Also, Zhejiang Chairman Zhang has sent a regiment of provincial defense forces to rush from Changshan to Yushan to assist in suppressing the communist bandits in eastern Jiangxi. (5) Various armies defeated the communist bandits. Brigade Commander Dai of the 18th Division, because Zhu Mao and Peng Huang were combining and had plans to attack Changsha again, supervised his troops to pursue the bandits. Also, Anfu was captured the other day. Division Commander Deng sent the 3rd Regiment to recover the county seat and escort Acting County Magistrate Wang Shaojie back to the county to handle the aftermath. Regiment Commander Wu of the 2nd Regiment of the police preparedness regiment recovered Xiajiang on August 25th. The bandits have fled far away.

Traffic Inside and Outside Shanhaiguan Gradually Restored 66

▲ Jilin-Beiping Joint Tickets on Sale

▲ Communication Line Between Fengtian and Tianjin Temporarily Used

Jilin dispatch: At the beginning of the month, the floods in western Liaoning caused great damage to the Beining Railway, and traffic inside and outside Shanhaiguan was interrupted for a long time. Trains between Beiping and Liaoning were not running. All passenger and freight traffic to and from the Northeast had to detour through Yingkou and Lianhe. Also, because the poles along the line were broken, telegrams were also cut off. Except for first-class official telegrams and third-class urgent telegrams, which could be sent via the Dalian water line and arrive on the same day, the rest, such as fourth-class commercial telegrams and reduced-price news telegrams, could only be sent to Yingkou, then mailed to Tianjin, and then forwarded, often arriving as late as four or five days or a week later, which was very inconvenient for merchants. It is now reported that the Beining Railway has been repaired and reopened on the 29th, without any obstacles. For the time being, one passenger train between Shenyang and Huai and one direct train between Shenyang and Beiping, as well as one freight train, will be opened daily. All roads in Jilin, Changchun, Jihai and Jitun have been approved by the road authorities to start selling Beiping joint tickets on the 30th. However, direct traffic between Jilin and Beiping will have to wait until the Beining Railway is fully restored before the date of traffic is discussed. The rumor that the traffic plan was cancelled is not true. According to news from the local telegraph bureau, the Beining telegraph line is being restored with great effort. The communication line between Fengtian and Tianjin has been repaired and perfected, and it will be used temporarily to transmit telegrams. From the 30th, it can be used without hindrance and does not need to be mailed through Yingkou. The 29th was the anniversary of the annexation of Japan and Korea. The authorities were deeply concerned that Koreans would cause trouble, and ordered the military and police in various places to be on strict alert in advance. As expected, on this day, a large number of bandits were found at the Liushuhe Station on the Jitun Railway, burning the stationmaster's office and killing many road workers. Later, because the military and police arrived in time, they were dispersed. The train still ran as usual, and there was no other damage. (August 30th)

Heilongjiang Province Comforts and Reassures Border Residents 67

Harbin dispatch: Along the upper reaches of the Heilongjiang River, from Mohe to Suibin, during the Russian military invasion last year, it was almost completely ravaged. The people were displaced and scattered, and the towns and villages became ruins. Although it seems that there are no Russian troops this year, Russian bandits are still active and constantly disrupting. For example, in Suibin, Luobei, Foshan, Wuyun, Qike, Aihun, Oupu, Huma, Mohe and other nine counties, merchants and residents have not fully returned to their hometowns. Huma, Mohe, Oupu, and Foshan counties have recently petitioned the provincial government to send troops to station there and to reorganize the border checkpoints to strengthen the frontier. At the same time, they also requested financial assistance to revive the business market. Therefore, the provincial government ordered Pang Guoguang, a specialist from the Secretariat, to go to the counties to investigate and comfort the people. At the same time, Wang Jingxiu, the chief of staff of the National Defense Preparatory Office, was ordered to go to the above-mentioned counties to inspect the border defense situation, investigate the Baojia and Karen situation, and then seek to improve the methods. Wang and Pang have already left yesterday, passing through Harbin. (August 31st)

Bandit Gang Returns and Another Kidnapping Case Occurs: Previously, the Tai Bao A Shu bandit gang entrenched itself in Liu Jia Yan Bridge and other places in this county, kidnapping, extorting, and committing all kinds of evil. The local people suffered greatly. Since they left for other places to rob on the 22nd of last month, the village has been slightly peaceful. Recently, it was heard that the bandit gang was defeated in the Zhang Lian Tang area of Jiashan County by the Jiahu Bandit Command, and it was thought that they could be somewhat suppressed. Unexpectedly, after the suppression by Re Gong, only more than ten people were killed and four were captured. Except for Pan Amu, who was killed on the spot, and Tai Bao A Shu, who was slightly injured, others such as Zhu Tan A Mei, Lu Heshang, and Yang Meimei were not injured. Therefore, although they suffered a small loss, their power has not diminished. Recently, these people have returned to their old nest in batches and are hiding in various places. When one batch of them returned, they happened to encounter the Pinghu-Shanghai Ban Xinqing Ferry near Xupu Tang, and stopped them for robbery, causing losses of more than 2,000 yuan. As a result, unrest has reappeared in the local area. After entering the room, they looted wantonly. When they left, they also took Gan Jinhai's nephew away, and placed a letter on the table, which stated (a ransom of 2,500 yuan, to be prepared within three days). Gan Hai was greatly shocked upon reading it, and it is not known whether he has prepared the ransom or not.

Jiading 72

People of Xu Gongqiao Petition for the Release of Wang Lin: Yesterday, Wang Lin, the principal of the Xu Gongqiao Central Primary School, was arrested by members of the Nanjing Garrison Command and handed over to the county government to be escorted to Beijing due to a case. Local people believed that Wang Lin had been in the school for more than a year, and his words and deeds were very cautious on weekdays. He was very enthusiastic about educating children. More than fifty local township chiefs and student families telegraphed the Central Party Department and Garrison Headquarters of the National Government in Nanjing, requesting his release after questioning. The text of the telegram is recorded as follows: To the Central Party Department and Garrison Headquarters of the National Government in Nanjing, Wang Lin, the principal of Xu Gongqiao Central Primary School, has been in office for more than a year, and has been focused on education. His words and deeds are peaceful, and he has gained the trust of the local people. He is content in his remote hometown and has no political odor. We were deeply shocked by his arrest yesterday. We, the residents, have lived here for generations and are living in peace. We are making this request out of conscience. If there are no special circumstances, we beg you to release him quickly. Township chiefs Jiang Daguang and Lu Huilan of Xu Gongqiao, Kunshan County, and student families Cai Huang, Zhang Cheng, etc., fifty-four people together kowtow in the sun.

A Swarm of Bees Almost Caused Trouble: Kunshan Xiaoxiong Bee Farm recently set up a branch farm in Zhangjing Township in the 8th District of this county, raising more than 130 boxes of bees. Every day at about 5:00 AM, they are released into the fields. The farmers in the township are not well-informed and consider the bees trampling the crops, and that the harvest will inevitably be damaged. They gathered to drive them away. Township Chief Wang Chengdong, fearing that it would cause trouble, tried his best to stop them, and at the same time reported to the district office for investigation. After receiving the report, District Chief Zhang sent a letter to the farm owner, inviting him to come to the office to discuss a proper solution. As a result, the farm owner guaranteed that if the place where the bees were released had a poorer harvest compared to other fields, he would be responsible, and he also publicized the benefits of beekeeping to the farmers. It was thus possible to avert the trouble invisibly.

Continued Investigation of the An Ting Murder Case: In the case of Fu Pinhua, a passenger at An Ting Railway Station, being injured, falling into the river, and dying, the county government detained the station porter Lu Jinzhang for interrogation. The entire staff of An Ting Railway Station, as well as the section chief of the East Section Car Affairs Section, telegraphed the Car Affairs Department separately, and the latter forwarded it to the Jinghu Railway Administration, which in turn sent a letter to the county government, inquiring about the reason for the detention of the porter. County Magistrate Chen has sent back the statements of the person who reported the case, the witness, and the corroborating evidence obtained from the investigation, stating that Fu Wangshi is indeed the wife of the deceased Fu Pinhua, and that Zhou Peirong and Qiao A'er are not go-betweens. Lu Jinzhang is highly suspected of causing the death of Fu Pinhua. A certain employee of the station and others are also related to the case and need to be interrogated according to the law. Stationmaster Zhou Xichen did not stop Lu's crime at the time, and later falsely accused the deceased's wife Fu Wangshi and Zhou Peirong and others of abduction. There is also a strong suspicion that he intentionally fabricated facts to cover up the perpetrator. The case should be handled according to the law. The Administration was notified. Also, Police Chief Zhu was ordered to take a document to Shanghai a few days ago to liaise with the Administration regarding this case and has returned to the county to report. The Administration also sent someone to An yesterday to investigate the facts. It is believed that there will be a solution to this case soon.

Wuxi 73

Change of Director of the Finance Bureau: Chen Liangdong, Director of the Finance Bureau, has repeatedly requested to resign to the Finance Department due to the extremely high local financial deficit and the actual difficulties in handling affairs. Chen, the director of the department, has approved his resignation. The vacancy will be filled by Zhuang Yeguang, who is recorded as a candidate for Director of the Finance Bureau. The matter has been submitted to the provincial government meeting for approval, and Director Chen has been ordered to expedite the handover.

Deterioration of Autumn Cocoon Information: Since the emergence of autumn cocoons in Wuxi last year, and with the best efforts of the silk cocoon industry in promoting them, farmers have generally recognized the benefits and raised a great deal of silkworms. However, the spring and summer cocoons of this year have been greatly affected by bad weather, and silk factories have deeply felt the pain of raw material shortage. Therefore, the promotion efforts have been particularly strong. The number of autumn silkworm eggs sold by various breeding farms is quite large. Unexpectedly, due to inconsistent weather, temperature, and the mixture of wind and rain, the silkworms have deteriorated, and the cocoons are of very low quality. Therefore, various manufacturers are wary. They specially convened a meeting of all industry members yesterday to discuss the matter. All agreed that the opening of the autumn cocoon market is imminent, but the cocoons this year are of low quality and the silk yield is particularly low. In order to maintain costs, various factories should be cautious in receiving goods to prevent losses. The resolution was passed by all members. As a result, various manufacturers have adopted a calm attitude towards the opening of the cocoon market. As of yesterday, the number of firms reporting their opening was less than one hundred.

Mass Education Committee and Cotton Mills Hold Important Meeting: The County Mass Education Committee convened yesterday a meeting of the executive and supervisory committee members of cotton mills such as Xin, Yu, Kangye, Qin, and Guangqin. The following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the issue of preventing reactionaries, the executive and supervisory committee members of the Mass Education Committee shall be responsible for effectively monitoring and immediately report any suspicious events or people to the county party headquarters. (2) Regarding the reorganization of the labor union, we will wait for the county party headquarters to send personnel to guide the reorganization according to the new law. (3) Regarding the issue of wages on revolutionary memorial days, the county party headquarters will urge the county government to strictly order the employers of various factories to promptly issue wages in accordance with the provincial order. (4) The county government will supervise the factories to implement the Factory Law.

Mediation of Dispute over the Construction of an Oil Tank: The Yuantai Petroleum Company previously built an oil tank outside the East Gate, which was opposed by nearby factories and residents who feared the danger of storing kerosene. The lawsuit has been going on for years without a resolution. After the opening of the Jiatai Silk Factory this year, the factory repeatedly petitioned the county government and the Construction Department to ban the oil tank because it was located next to the silk factory. Yesterday, the Construction Department instructed the county government to notify the County Chamber of Commerce and the parties concerned to hold a meeting in the county to mediate the dispute on the 12th of this month.

Another Robbery Case Reported in Kaihua Township: Recently, robbery cases have been occurring frequently in the four townships of this county. Although the authorities have been strictly pursuing and arresting the bandits, very few cases have been solved, which has emboldened the bandits and made them extremely rampant. Yesterday, in Nianqi Situ Dianli Lane, Kaihua Township, the home of Hui Jizhu was robbed by six or seven bandits who climbed over the wall and entered the house. They robbed 500 yuan in silver dollars and all valuables, with total losses reaching 1,000 yuan. A certain long-term worker of the Hui family was tied up with a rope, hung up, and severely beaten, resulting in injuries all over his body and inability to move.

Execution of Four Kidnapping Bandits: Shi Yaogen, son of Shi Lansheng of Youguang Bridge outside the East Gate of Jiaxing, was kidnapped by bandits on April 25th of this year. The Provincial Public Security Bureau later arrested the bandits Chen Peisheng, Shou Xing, Yang Ziming, Wang A Si, Ma Xin Chang, Pu Ruan Shi, etc. in the Puyuan Township area of Puyang's family. Zhang Yousong was found in the cellar and sent to the Provincial Government Security Department for interrogation. They had previously kidnapped Yao Gen, son of Shi Lansheng of Youguang Bridge, and hid him in the same cellar, eventually extorting 5,000 yuan. Ma Xin Chang confessed that he only watched the treasury for one day, and his circumstances were relatively minor. He and Pu Ruan Shi were sentenced to imprisonment separately. The other four, Chen Peisheng, Shou Xing, Shou Ziming, and Wang A Si, were sentenced to death as usual. On September 5th, the provincial government escorted the bandits to Wei and then to Youguang Bridge for execution by firing squad.

County Public Security Bureau Chief Transferred: Mo Runxun, Chief of the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau, was ordered to be transferred to Chief of the Shaoxing County Public Security Bureau, and Shen Weihan, Director of the Second District of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, was transferred to take over as Chief of the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau. Huzhou 80

Bandits Demand Extortion and Prevent Tenants from Harvesting Rice: Tao Yongji, a resident of Dongzhang Wang Temple across the river from Hongxing Bridge in Changxing, has a wealth of assets and has long been coveted by bandits. Because of the rampant banditry, Tao moved to Changyi two years ago, renting out all his fields and only collecting interest. On the 26th of last month, seven or eight bandits suddenly arrived at the homes of Tao's tenants, ordering them to inform Tao that he had to borrow 40,000 yuan and pay it quickly. Tao ignored the message after hearing about it. Unexpectedly, at 7:00 PM on the 2nd of this month, the bandits who had demanded the extortion told the tenants that if Tao did not pay 40,000 yuan, they would not be allowed to harvest their rice, or else. However, the tenants' livelihoods depend on the autumn harvest, so the tenants are all worried.

Bandits Rob Accounting Boat in Dongqiao Village: In Dongqiao Village near Yangjia Zhuang outside the West Gate of this city, at about 3:00 PM on the 4th, six bandits speaking a foreign accent were seen looking around along the river. An accounting boat from Yuanfeng Distillery in this city happened to be passing by after collecting more than 300 yuan from Meixi and Heping. The bandits saw the boat coming and immediately took out their pistols, shouting for the boat to stop. The bandits jumped onto the boat and robbed all the money.

It has been ten days since the incident. His brother Yan Fagen learned of the incident at home and immediately rushed to draft a lawsuit, continuing to ask the County Court to severely punish the murderer Zhu A Huan to seek justice.

Meeting Held to Draft Soldiers: The Xiaoshan County Government received an order from the province to draft soldiers. On August 27th, a meeting was convened of village chiefs and deputy chiefs to discuss the matter. It was resolved that one soldier would be drafted for every 100 households and sent to the county before September 15th. Now that the deadline is approaching, Xu Yuanzhang, the head of the First District Public Office, together with Gao Shichun, Chief of the Public Security Bureau, notified the village chiefs to convene another temporary meeting at 2:00 PM on September 6th to resolve the issue of drafting soldiers.

Hefei 83

Private Arms Smuggling Case to Be Investigated: Li Buzhou and Huang Shuifu were caught smuggling 21 firearms and hundreds of rounds of ammunition at Sancha River and sent to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters for detention. Letters

Letter from Ma Tianmin 84

In yesterday's local news column of your newspaper, there was a Suzhou news item stating that "Ma Canmin committed suicide in an inn." After verification, many of the facts are inconsistent. I used to be the chief translator of the Great Li Lawyer's Office. After the recovery of the Mixed Court in the Concession, I retired and lived in seclusion, studying law. I have been sick for many years, taking medicine, staying at home, and making a living frugally. I have never served in the army, nor have I dared to hope to be rich. My younger brother, Wen Chao (also known as Canmin), has not been engaged in proper business in recent years and has been addicted to gambling. He has been repeatedly warned but has not repented. This time, he gambled again and used my name to solicit money everywhere (after the fact, it was discovered that there were many cases of fraudulently collecting money). He attempted to make a profit but was ashamed to see people, so he ran away. Before leaving, he took away antique calligraphy and paintings worth 180 yuan and pawned them for 6 gold. He went to Suzhou to take poison and was rescued, almost faking his death to make a joke of it. Otherwise, would he not have a place to die in Shanghai? My younger brother is young and ignorant, and his will is weak, as all relatives and friends know. I am concerned about my brother and cannot ignore him. My strict supervision has caused resentment. The claim that he committed suicide due to family pressure is not true. This matter concerns my reputation, and I cannot remain silent. Moreover, I am afraid that the outside world does not know the truth and will easily misunderstand. Therefore, I have briefly stated the situation and ask for a correction. I would be grateful. Ma Tianmin, September 6th.

Special Article

Report on the Participation of the National Private Electricity Industry Association in the World Power Conference (Continued) 85

Li Yanshi, Shen Sifang

(1) Liaison with Electricity Industry Associations of Various Countries, Inquiry about Their Organizational Status, and Exchange of Views on Association Affairs: The United Kingdom, France, Germany, Switzerland, and other countries all have sound organizations. The United Kingdom has a total of four electricity industry associations, one organized by sixteen large companies, one organized by ten commercial companies near London, one organized by small and medium-sized power plants across the country, and one organized by municipal power plants in various cities. The affairs of the French Electricity Industry Association are also very developed. The International Electricity Industry Association is located there. The German Electricity Industry Association has the most complete and developed organization. In addition to commercial companies, municipal power plants are also involved, and the combination of government and business is rare. Switzerland also has a spirit. (2) The Process of Joining the International Electricity Industry Association: When Yanshi and others were investigating in Switzerland, they learned that the International Electricity Industry Association was located in Paris. Through the introduction of the Swiss Electricity Industry Association, they met with the association's secretary, Berlin Sky, and learned that the association had been established for three years and had more than forty members. In mid-September of this year, the annual meeting was held in Beijing. Knowing that Yanshi and others represented the Chinese private electricity industry, they expressed their welcome and invited them to join the association and attend the meeting in Beijing. Because the annual meeting of our association was approaching, Yanshi and others had to return to China and requested Fei Futao to attend the meeting nearby. From then on, the Chinese electricity industry and the industry of various countries in the world will be united and will surely flourish in the future. (3) The Process of Contacting Various Manufacturing Factories: Due to overproduction and sluggish sales in various European countries, especially Germany, Yanshi and others visited various factories in Germany, such as the United Steel Company, Ai Yiji Siemens Electric Manufacturing Factory, Daoci Linkhoff Mentel Diesel Engine Manufacturing Factory, and the Swiss Bulangbi Electric Manufacturing Factory and Huajia Electric Meter Manufacturing Factory, all warmly welcomed and expressed their willingness to cooperate with this association, providing convenience to all colleagues. The consumer cooperation business of this association can be established. (4) Collection of Electrical Regulations and Statistical Reports of Various Countries: This time, wherever Yanshi and others went, the statistical annual reports and regulations regarding the electrical industry were collected very richly. The current situation of the electricity industry in various countries and the legal status of electrical enterprises became clearer. Most of the electricity industries in France are jointly operated by the city and business, and fewer are commercially operated. However, the state has constitutional provisions to protect commercial operations in a comprehensive manner. The following is an excerpt from Article 153 of the Constitution: Private property is guaranteed by the Constitution. When private property is requisitioned for public interest, a fair price must be compensated in accordance with the provisions of the law. In case of disputes, the decision must be made by the High Court. When the central government levies property from the local government, it must also pay a fair price. The British electrical regulations are even more comprehensive. Previously, the operating period of the British electricity industry was only twenty years. Later, due to various inconveniences, it was changed to forty years. Today, sixteen large electrical companies across the country have obtained permanent operating rights. Except for the Soviet government of Russia, the electricity industry is either commercially operated or municipally operated, or jointly operated by the city and business. There are no central government agencies directly operating. Although there is one factory in Germany directly under the central government, it is located near a coal mine, which is inconvenient for transportation and is used to generate electricity and sell it to various electrical companies, and is not directly operated. (5) Comparison of Electricity Prices in Various Countries: This time, from Nanyang India to Europe, we visited more than ten countries, visited factories, contacted association affairs, and visited friends. At the same time, we conducted on-site inspections of electricity prices and equipment conditions. Currently, various business regulations and statistical charts are on the way, and only the memories can be briefly described to know the outline. The business regulations of the Little Luzon Power Company are very complete. The method of pricing is divided into area fees. The minimum area of each room is 50 square meters, and the monthly fee is one peso. Above 50 square meters, an additional 20 points are charged for every 20 square meters. The electricity fee is 15 points per degree within 15 degrees, and gradually decreases above that. For example, if a small user uses 10 degrees of electricity per month, the price is 25 points per degree, which is equivalent to 5 cents in Chinese currency. In the Medan area of Dutch India, the price of electricity is 45 points per degree. The currency system in that area is roughly the same as Chinese currency. In Berlin, Germany, the price of electricity is 50 points per degree regardless of the base degree, and 20 points per degree for those with a base degree. Small users, including the base degree, cost between 1.8 and 1.9 cents in Chinese currency per degree. Also, according to a friend in the suburbs, the monthly electricity consumption is 75 degrees, and the price is 15 points per degree plus the base degree, which is 24 points per degree. In Hamburg, the price is 45 points per degree. In Switzerland, the price of electricity is divided into three levels: the highest is 50 points, the middle is 20 points, and the lowest is 7 points. The table rent is 7.5 Swiss francs per quarter. For the St. Paul Malle Company in London, the price of electricity is 4 pence per degree for annual consumption within 2,000 degrees, and the table rent is a minimum of 1 kilowatt, which is 2 shillings and 6 pence per quarter. For small and medium-sized users, the price is 5 pence per degree. The price of electricity for small and medium-sized power plants in China is more than one shilling per degree, and the power is more than 8 pence per degree. These power plants are larger than most of our large power plants in China. In the Li Ai Ji area of Belgium, the price of electricity is 2.2 francs per degree, plus table rent, etc., which is about 2.7 cents in Chinese currency per degree. In Moscow, Russia, the price of electricity is 18 kopecks per degree, which is equivalent to 3.6 cents in Chinese currency. From this point of view, the large cities of various countries have a large population, prosperous commerce, and a large power generation capacity of power plants, which are dozens or hundreds of times that of the average power plants in our country. The price is more expensive and is not available in our country. The price of electricity in our country is either the cheapest in the world or one of the cheapest. (6) Conversations with Various Experts: (A) University Professor and Electrical Expert Demai, who is the electrical commissioner of the recent German industrial inspection team to China, said that the joint operation of the electrical industry by the city and business is most suitable for the modern trend. However, China's politics is not yet on track, and officialdom is not yet clear, so it is not yet possible to talk about it, so commercial operation is still preferable. He also said that there are three prerequisites for Germany and China to cooperate in developing industry: first, to be realistic; second, to abide by the law; and third, to provide adequate guarantees. For the development of China's electrical industry, it is advocated to start with building more small-scale power plants. If large-scale power plants are built first, there is no need for them at present, and when the need is reached in the future, the machine styles and economic conditions will no longer be suitable. (B) Long Fu, Secretary of the German Electricity Industry Association and Doctor of Law, said that the association's members account for 95% of the total power generation capacity of all power plants in the country, regardless of whether they are municipal or commercial. The association is the only organization that connects the government and the people. Government policies are often implemented due to the mediation of the association. He also said that the German electrical industry is not worried about illegal administrative punishment due to the provisions of the Constitution. When commercially operated companies are transferred to municipal operation, the value of their wealth-generating and operating areas is estimated, and they are handled fairly and cash is issued, which often exceeds the face value. The takeover of the Berlin power plant by the city is one example. (C) Banker and Economic Doctor Nabro said that Germany's current difficulties are no less than those of China, and it relies entirely on foreign capital to survive. However, it is down-to-earth and trustworthy, so it can continue to turn around. Without credit, it would have been unimaginable long ago. China is currently affected by the high price of gold and the low price of silver and should vigorously promote production and export in order to balance the import and export of cash. Otherwise, there is no solution. (To be continued)

Education News and Highlights

Ministry of Education Orders Appropriate Reduction and Exemption of Tuition Fees for Students from Shaanxi, Gansu, Chahar, and Suiyuan 86

Nanjing, 6th: The Ministry of Education believes that the four provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Chahar, and Suiyuan are suffering from natural disasters and man-made disasters, and the economy is in a state of panic. Students studying abroad are having difficulty with their fees. It has issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, ordering them to instruct schools at all levels to identify students from the four provinces and appropriately reduce or exempt their tuition fees for this year to show compassion.

Beijing Municipal Party Headquarters

Request to Cancel University Vice-Presidents, etc. 87

Nanjing, 6th: The Beijing Municipal Party Headquarters believes that the current national universities do not have the titles of vice-president, dean of academic affairs, secretary-general, etc., which are inconsistent with the current university organization law. Moreover, the presidents of various schools therefore hold only empty titles, travel abroad, causing internal disputes and wasting students' studies. It will submit a letter to the Central Government requesting a strict order to cancel these titles to respect the law and maintain academics.

Training Headquarters Plans

Striving for Foreign Language Education 88

▲Regulations Promulgated to All Military Organs, Schools, and the Training Directorate General. The Directorate General held a working meeting at 9:00 AM the other day to discuss various urgent matters. The meeting was chaired by Deputy Director Zhou Yawei. The discussion items included: 1. Proposal to establish a military academic research association; 2. Proposal to organize a foreign language research association; 3. Other proposals (still in progress). The meeting also passed a proposal to promote foreign language education in all military organs, schools, and units, which is excerpted below. Proposal to promote foreign language education in all military organs, schools, and units: Given the global advancements in transportation and science, foreign languages serve as a tool for gathering a wide range of knowledge and a medium for absorbing new information. While studying abroad requires proficiency in the language to achieve effective results, even within the country, the ability to read foreign books and newspapers is essential for expanding knowledge and understanding military affairs. Since the end of the European war, military academics have undergone rapid changes. However, due to the scarcity of military personnel proficient in foreign languages in our country, the translated works of new books are rare, and widespread access to military affairs in various countries is difficult to achieve. Even selecting personnel for overseas study in the hope of learning from others is ineffective without qualified personnel proficient in the language of the study destination. Therefore, promoting foreign language education is a matter of utmost urgency. A summary of measures is proposed below for public decision. (Measures for promoting foreign language education in all military organs, schools, and units): 1. All military organs, schools, and units must ensure that military officers who have already learned a foreign language practice regularly to avoid becoming rusty and find ways to improve their proficiency. Those who have not learned a foreign language must be encouraged to learn. 2. All military organs and units, to promote foreign language education, should encourage officers to conduct self-study or set up remedial classes, assigning officers already proficient in a particular foreign language to provide guidance, without adhering to rigid formalities, but aiming to achieve this goal through various methods. 3. All army schools should add foreign language courses for cadets and students, and all instructors should either attend remedial classes with the students or establish separate research associations to implement this. 4. Foreign languages are temporarily limited to English, Russian, French, German, and Japanese. Each organ, unit, and school should adopt one or more languages, depending on its needs and practical circumstances. 5. Foreign language education and research, in addition to ordinary methods, should pay special attention to listening, note-taking, and military terminology. 6. Each unit and school under the headquarters should, at the end of each year, report to the headquarters on the foreign language research situation of all officers, cadets, and students for assessment. Those who are capable of translation and direct listening should be carefully reported according to the following investigation form for reference. Military organs can also follow these guidelines for their subordinates. 7. Foreign Language Education Investigation Form (Form omitted).

Reorganization and Establishment of the Guangdong Academy of Law 93

The Guangdong Academy of Law, formerly known as the Guangdong Judges Academy, was founded by the Premier during his tenure as Grand Marshal in 1924. Initially, it was directly under the jurisdiction of the Guangdong Higher Court and the Procuratorate. In 1926, when the former Judicial Yuan was in Guangdong, the president was once dismissed, and a committee system was adopted, with all members appointed by the ministry. After the Ministry of Justice moved to Wuhan, the old system was restored. A total of 297 students have graduated, and 762 students have studied at the academy, with excellent results. This time, the Ministry of Judicial Administration ordered the academy to be reorganized into an Academy of Law in accordance with the University Organization Law. Since it was reorganized into a national academy, it does not conflict with the resolution of the Second Plenary Session of the Third Central Executive Committee regarding the central and local judicial administrative organs or courts not establishing educational institutions similar to judge training schools. Although the Ministry of Judicial Administration believes that the issue of affiliation should, in principle, be under the direct jurisdiction of the Ministry of Education, the school was founded by the Premier and has been affiliated with judicial organs for a long time, with special historical circumstances. Therefore, it has consulted the Ministry of Education and intends to have the academy directly under the Ministry of Judicial Administration, with all matters such as the appointment of the president handled by the Ministry of Judicial Administration. (After the reorganization, it was established on July 21 this year, and the Ministry of Judicial Administration ordered the Guangdong Higher Court to appoint Yao Lixiu as the president. Yao graduated from Tokyo Hosei University in Japan and was sworn in on July 21.) It still requests the Ministry of Education for record. The Ministry of Education recently replied to the Ministry of Judicial Administration, stating that it has received the report from the National Guangdong Academy of Law regarding the reorganization and establishment of the academy and the date of the president's inauguration, requesting for record, and attached a resume, which has been passed to the ministry. It should be filed for record immediately. However, in accordance with the Measures for Unified Education Administration resolved at the Eighth Meeting of the Executive Yuan in 1929 (all schools and cultural undertakings, except for party affairs schools, military schools, and research institutes of the Academia Sinica, regardless of which organ establishes or conducts them, should report the educational part in detail to the Ministry of Education and be subject to the supervision and guidance of the Ministry of Education), a corresponding reply is given, hoping that your ministry will comply and report everything from time to time for reference.

Local News

Shanghai Education Bureau Reforms Public Education Centers 96

The Shanghai Education Bureau will reorganize the internal organization of the public education centers established by the bureau from the 19th year onwards in order to maximize the effectiveness of dynamic education. The plan, drafted by the head of the section, Chen Duanzhi, has been submitted for discussion and approved by Director Chen, who has instructed all education centers to follow it. The reorganization plan is excerpted below. This bureau, after four months of trial in November of the 17th year, observed the practical needs and created public tea gardens. During the period of political tutelage, school education and social education are equally important, and the place for educating the public has to resort to the tea gardens of the recreation center. This is how the public tea gardens came into being. After a year of operation, it was generally believed that the reorganization of public tea gardens into tea gardens for the public was restrictive for the progress of the cause. Therefore, in November of the 18th year, a separate building was found to set up a simple public education center in order to implement the plan for public education. In the past six months, according to the research of this bureau and the reports of various directors, although it is slightly better than the public tea gardens, it is still far from the plan of this bureau. Now that the beginning of the year is approaching, the internal organization will be reorganized to maximize the effectiveness of dynamic education. The reorganization plan is listed below. (1) The internal organization of the public education center: 1. Newspaper and Book Department: Display popular libraries and purchase daily newspapers for public reading and learning. 2. Entertainment Department: Select and purchase entertainment equipment to cultivate the public's interest and habits in legitimate recreation. 3. Communication Department: Use correspondence and face-to-face inquiry methods to resolve the public's daily doubts. 4. Propaganda Department: Hold various popular lectures to guide the public's knowledge and skills in daily life. (2) Regulations on the duties of directors: 1. Lectures: Hold regular and circuit lectures on daily and occasional matters. 2. Guidance: Provide separate guidance on all matters in daily life. 3. Visits: Go deep into the people to connect emotions and understand the people's concerns. 4. Investigation: Conduct simple investigations to create simple statistics so that the public has the concept of comparing weights. (3) Revision of forms (omitted).

Sports

Shanghai Foreign Football Club Report 101

丨Describing the Situation from 1929 to 1930丨

▲Continuous Rain During the Competition Period Extended the Order

▲Excellent Results for Each Team, Fortuna Unfortunately Lost the Championship

▲The All Nations Cup Charity Match in the Middle Has Not Been Rescheduled

Mr. Hamson, Honorary Secretary of the Shanghai Foreign Football Club, distributed the general report on the club's progress from 1929 to 1930 to various sectors. The more important parts are recorded below.

The football season of 1929 to 1930 can be said to be very successful. The difficulty felt was the interference of the rain, which often hindered the competition and extended the original schedule, which was not completed until the fourth week of April. In addition, the club's executives often found it difficult to allocate referees. Captain Graham of the British Army, who had refereeing experience, assisted the club a great deal with his experience, and the referees' dedicated service was very effective.

▲Interport Matches This year's Interport Matches were held in Shanghai. Tianjin and Hong Kong arrived in Shanghai as scheduled. Shanghai was very lucky and defeated Hong Kong and Tianjin to win the championship. The results are as follows:

Date Winner Score Loser Score

February 1 Shanghai Team 5 Hong Kong Team 2

February 2 Shanghai Team 3 Tianjin Team 2

February 3 Hong Kong Team 3 Tianjin Team 2

There were also friendly matches at the time. The results of the rainy pitch are recorded below:

Date Winner Score Loser Score

February 6 British Army 7 Tianjin Team 4

February 7 British Army 6 Hong Kong Team 3

▲Division A Competition Eight teams participated. Fortuna and Wanderers competed most fiercely. Fortuna lost by one point and was ranked second. Wanderers played 13 times and achieved excellent results. Suddenly, they left Shanghai before the end. In the last match, Greenhua replaced them and completed the great feat. The results of each team are as follows:

Team Name Matches Wins Draws Losses Goals Scored Goals Conceded Points

Greenhua 14 11 1 1 78 20 24

Fortuna 14 10 3 1 50 25 23

Shanghai Customs 14 9 0 5 56 29 18

Western Police 14 7 1 6 39 35 15

Shanghai 14 6 1 7 51 49 13

Lacksters 14 4 2 8 31 53 10

Shanghai Dockyards 14 4 1 9 31 64 9

Portuguese 14 0 0 14 19 79 0

▲Division B Competition Division B was divided into two groups, A and B. Ten teams participated in Division B A, with St. Francis Xavier taking the lead. Eleven teams participated in Division B B, with the Jewish team taking the lead.

▲Scott Cup Thirteen teams participated. Fortuna was one of them. The knockout system was adopted. Fortuna competed twice with the Shanghai Municipal Police for the final. The first time was a 3-3 draw. The second time, Fortuna was defeated 1-5. In the final, the Shanghai team defeated the Western Police 5-4 and won the cup championship.

▲Senior Cup Fortuna was one of the eight teams competing for the cup. Unfortunately, they were defeated by Wanderers 2-3 in the semi-finals. As a result, Wanderers defeated the long-time champion Wanderers 3-2 and won the championship.

▲Nations Cup Eight countries participated in the war, including China, England, Portugal, Germany, France, Jewish, and Scotland. After several bloody battles, China, England, Scotland, and Portugal won the semi-final rights. Later, China defeated England 2-0, and Scotland defeated Portugal 2-1, and got the final right. In the final, China and Scotland competed for the championship. China won 2-0 and won the cup championship.

▲Other Competitions The results of other competitions such as the Zilong Cup and the Junior Cup are that the former championship was won by St. Francis Xavier, and the latter belonged to the Navy. As for the Sino-Western Charity Match, whether to abandon it due to two unfinished matches or to hold another match will be resolved by the new staff.

Finally, the club expressed its deep gratitude to the enthusiastic people who participated in the club, such as Mr. Hao Boyang, Secretary General of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation, and Captain Stephen of the British Army.
