Local News Two

Zhu Ruchao, a Shopkeeper Involved in the Hundred Thousand Yuan Robbery, Commits Suicide 173

▲Suffered a Nervous Breakdown After the Case

▲Attempted Suicide in the Huangpu River Three Days Ago, Was Rescued

▲Cut His Throat with a Kitchen Knife Behind Someone's Back Yesterday Morning

▲Admitted to the Hospital, Life in Danger

The hundred thousand yuan robbery case has been going on for ten days. Since the huge sum was robbed on August 28th, the police have been making every effort to investigate. Three days later, several suspects involved in the case were arrested one after another, sent to the public court, and confessed to the robbery. The details have been recorded in previous reports. However, at around 4:30 AM yesterday morning, Zhu Ruchao, a shopkeeper from the Zhejiang Local Bank in Hangzhou who had escorted the hundred thousand yuan to Shanghai, suddenly committed suicide at the Donglai Bank, cutting his throat with a sharp blade, and his life is in danger. After the case was solved, part of the stolen money has been recovered. Now that Zhu Ruchao suddenly commits suicide, the case has taken another strange turn. Although no one dares to speculate on the reasons for his seeking death, Zhu is nearly sixty years old and has been serving at the Zhejiang Local Bank for nearly seventeen years. Now that he has met with an unexpected disaster and had the intention of dying a violent death, it is indeed tragic.

▲Attempted Suicide by Drowning, But Was Rescued. Zhu Ruchao, the shopkeeper, has been temporarily residing at the Donglai Bank at No. 407 Henan Road since the case occurred, so that the police could question him at any time. However, since being shocked on the way on the 28th, his nerves have been greatly stimulated. He often mutters to himself, walks unsteadily, and lowers his head without speaking. Even those who try to comfort him are ignored. Three days ago, Zhu took advantage of the lack of attention and went to the Huangpu River to drown himself. Fortunately, a passerby saw him and rescued him, preventing him from suffering a violent death. After this incident occurred, the bank, fearing that Zhu's behavior would cause complications, immediately telegraphed Shaoxing, instructing his son to come to Shanghai to take care of him. Who knew that a major disaster would suddenly occur three days later?

▲Suicide by Kitchen Knife. At around 4:30 AM yesterday morning, when it was still dark, Zhu suddenly crept out of his bedroom and went to the kitchen, where he selected the sharpest kitchen knife. He went to the iron gate at the back of the Donglai Bank, facing Tianjin Road, and cut his throat. At this time, the bank's staff and servants were all asleep and did not know anything about it. Even the watchman, a Chinese constable, was sound asleep and did not know about the disaster that was happening. Suddenly, a tea servant sleeping on the second floor heard a cry of agony, lingering in his ears. He felt very strange and listened carefully, realizing that the sound came from downstairs, near the street. He called his companions, put on his clothes, and went downstairs to see what was going on.

▲Terrified the Child. After Zhu cut himself, he fell to the ground in pain, groaning. The first to be awakened by the sound was the cook's son. He slipped on his shoes and followed the sound, seeing Zhu lying under the iron gate at the entrance of the lane, his hands and feet struggling on the ground. His white hair and red blood reflected under the lamplight, and his face was hideous and terrifying. The child was greatly frightened and ran inside, and the people upstairs gathered at this time, asking what happened and panicking. They rushed to Zhu's side, seeing him naked from the waist up, wearing pants, the knife on the ground, the blade covered in blood, a hole in his head, and blood flowing out. They quickly reported to the police and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment.

▲Esophagus Severed. When he was sent to the hospital, he was already unconscious due to excessive blood loss. The doctor found that his esophagus had been severed, the wound was three inches wide and two inches deep, and his life was in great danger. Especially because he was old and weak and his nerves were unstable, it was feared that he would not recover. His son received the telegram sent by the Donglai Bank in the morning and came to Shanghai on the noon train to take care of his father. It is said that although Zhu is nearly sixty years old, his parents are still alive and in their eighties.

Xu MaoYun

Looks Like a Bandit Leader 174

▲Dong Shufang Mistakenly Reported to the Police

▲Realized It Was Not Him After Careful Examination

▲Both Were Released After Questioning and Judgment

In Ganyu County, Jiangbei, there is a man named Xu Dingxin, nicknamed "Fourth Master," who is a well-known local tyrant in the county. Although he is already in his sixties, his wild nature of bullying and oppressing the good and weak in the countryside has not changed slightly due to his age. He has many followers, and many nearby bandits are under his command, so his power is not weak. In the spring of the seventeenth year, the county government and the party department presented a petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Provincial Party Department to offer a large reward for the arrest of Xu by all military and police agencies. In February of that year, Wang Guangsha, the director of the Overseas Public Security Bureau, purchased information and arrested Xu. Wang went to the provincial capital to request instructions on the procedure for sending him to the province for handling. Unexpectedly, Xu was very powerful and secretly sent a message to his gang after Wang entered the province, and they dared to gather a crowd to rob the prison and take Xu away. From then on, he disappeared, and Wang's success was almost punished. He then resigned. On July 23 of this year, a large number of bandits suddenly arrived in Yujiawan, Ganyu County, armed with complete equipment, led by Xu, and looted at will, killing and setting fire, doing everything evil. Dong Shufang's family in the area suffered a great loss. This was because Dong's uncle, Dong Xuepei, was a member of the Ganyu County Party Department in the spring of the seventeenth year. Xu believed that he was wanted by the government because of Dong Xuepei's denunciation, so he hated Dong to the bone. This time, he gathered bandits from all directions to harm Yujiawan, with the purpose of obtaining Dong Xuepei to avenge the old hatred. Therefore, the Dong family was devastated the most. Dong Shufang dared not live at home and fled to Shanghai to seek refuge. He recently received a home report saying that after Xu Dingxin looted Yujiawan with his gang and divided the spoils, he had fled to Shanghai because the local military and police were investigating strictly. Dong then paid special attention when going out, hoping to meet him, and then send him to the government for punishment, so as to eliminate the scourge of the people. At 11:00 AM the day before yesterday, Dong saw an old man on the road whose shape resembled Xu Dingxin. He followed him to Maijiaquan, Shandong Road. The old man entered the Huizhong Hotel there, and Dong followed him in. After inquiring, he learned that the old man was indeed a guest of Huizhong, living in room 58. Although the name of the guest on the nameplate was not Xu Dingxin, the origin and age were mostly the same. He thought that the bandit had deliberately changed his name. When he wanted to report to the police, he was troubled by his unfamiliarity, so he knew that Wang Guangsha was still in Shanghai, so he went to visit Wang, asking him to accompany him to the General Patrol House, reported the information, and asked the police to arrest him immediately. Western Detective Mei Sheng asked him again and again, and Dong insisted that the old man was indeed the notorious bandit Xu Dingxin, without any doubt. If the information was found to be false in the future, he was willing to accept the punishment. Detective Mei then went to room 58 of the Huizhong Hotel with Chinese detectives Wang Shunlin and Ma Wenda, and Dong and Wang. The old man was in the room, with a servant serving him. Detective Mei asked Dong again, and Dong still said that the old man was a notorious bandit. So the Chinese and Western detectives arrested the master and servant. Unexpectedly, Dong suddenly said that it was a mistake, because after careful examination of the old man's appearance, although it was roughly similar to the Xu bandit, there were still dissimilarities. Detective Mei heard Dong's words and thought that Dong had made a very hasty judgment. Since he had stated in advance that he would investigate the facts, he brought Dong and Wang, along with the old man and his servant, back to the police station. After questioning, he learned that the old man's name was Xu Maohan, a salt merchant from Haizhou, and he was sixty-two years old. His servant, Li Shun, was also from the same hometown. Only the surname and age of the old man were the same as the Xu bandit Dong had mentioned. Even more strange was that he also had the nickname "Fourth Master." Yang Huo's appearance was similar to Confucius, and it can be seen that the similarity of human appearances is true in both ancient and modern times. Yesterday morning, the police sent the four people to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Xu Bolong opened the court for interrogation. After the police lawyer Ru Baoyi explained the process, and that this matter was not an intentional false accusation, Dong was only caused by the banditry his family suffered, and Wang only accompanied Dong to the police station. It was proposed that no charges be filed against the two people's misunderstandings. Judge Xu then asked Dong and others one by one, and then ordered Xu Maoyun, Li Shun, Dong Shufang, and Wang Guangsha to be released, and also told Xu and Li that if they wanted to sue Dong, they could file a complaint themselves.

Kidnapping of Huang Bohui 175

▲Sentencing Scheduled for Next Saturday

▲Witnesses Interrogated Again Yesterday

The kidnapping of Mr. Huang Bohui, the manager of the Shibao, was resolved when the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's water and land detectives rescued Mr. Huang on a bandit boat in western Shanghai within seven hours, and captured Zhou Wu and Li Wang, two people guarding the hostage, and seized a pistol. Because the incident occurred in the Public Concession, the Public Security Bureau extradited them to the Special District Local Court for interrogation. The details have been reported previously. The trial continued yesterday morning. The two pistols seized have also been handed over by the Public Security Bureau to the police station for investigation. Yu Bingfang, the boy who was sleeping in Mr. Huang's car at the time, testified that he was sleeping in the car that night to cool off, and he fell asleep. Later, the bandits drove the car to Singapore Road and then drove him off. The bandits hired a rickshaw to take him back to report the news, but he could not recognize the faces of the bandits. Zhou Jinx, a worker at the Shibao, testified that he was cooling off in the alley at the time when he heard the police whistle and ran out of the alley, knowing that the owner had been kidnapped. He chased after the car, but because he was unable to walk fast, it was difficult to catch up with the bandit car, and he could not recognize the faces of the bandits. Judge Xu then questioned the two defendants and appointed lawyer Yuan Hanyun to defend the defendants. After the debate ended, the court ordered the defendants to be returned to custody separately, and the sentencing was scheduled for Saturday morning.

Continued Trial of the Patricide Case 176

▲Ji Shuangquan Has Someone to Testify

▲Qiu Lan's Eating Snails Not Established

The case of Sun Laowu, a native of Nantong in Quxia Bridge, Zhabei, being killed by his adopted son Sun Liansheng in collusion with Ji Shuangquan, Qiu Lansheng, and Qiu Shunlong, etc., has been prosecuted by the local court. Sun Liansheng has confessed to how he planned and killed, etc. However, Ji Shuangquan, Qiu Lansheng, etc. still do not admit it and have presented evidence to testify. For the sake of caution, Chief Judge Chen Bingrong of the Criminal Court continued the trial yesterday to seek more details. According to Wang Da, the witness of Ji Shuangquan, Ji Shuangquan was at his home for a bidding meeting around 7:00 PM on the second day of June. However, Qiu Lansheng claimed that he was eating snails at home at 7:30 PM on the second day of June and did not go to kill anyone. Later, after questioning his father, Qiu Changfu, he said that he had not eaten snails. Shao Songchun, who lived next door, was the person Qiu Lansheng named as having eaten snails with him, but Shao also denied eating snails, saying that he was already asleep at 7:00 PM and heard Zhang the carpenter go to Qiu Lansheng's house around 8:00 PM, and Qiu Lansheng was not yet asleep. The court then asked the plaintiff, Sun Fusheng, whether the clothes of Sun Liansheng and Qiu Shuntao when they were arrested were the same as now, and he replied yes. The court then carefully examined the clothes and found no blood stains. Therefore, the judge asked Sun Fusheng to invite the neighbor of the deceased to court to state the situation, and if he was unwilling to come to court, he should submit a written statement to be attached to the case. The case was postponed for debate, and the court ordered the defendants to be returned to custody.

Wen Linsen's Suicide Note 177

▲Oppressed by Family Environment

▲Had No Choice But to Commit Suicide

Wen Linsen, a native of Shanghai living in the triangle area of Xujiahui, French Concession, was twenty-one years old this year. He lost his father at a young age. His father, Wen Dongsheng, ran a barber shop in Japan. After his father's death, his mother, Jiang, became familiar with Yao Yueting and supported the shop. Yao died last year. Linsen came of age and learned to be a water pipe fitter. Recently, due to disagreements between mother and son, they often quarreled. Linsen had a sudden idea and went out on the evening of the 4th to check into room 19 of the Gongshang Hotel at No. 313 Xinxiao Bridge Street, where he secretly swallowed raw opium and committed suicide. By noon the next day, the tea boy saw him sleeping and not getting up, called him but did not respond, pried open the door and went inside to check, and Wen had died of suffocation. The hotel reported to the Daximingzhong Police Station and ordered detectives to carry the body to the Tongren Fuyuantang autopsy for examination. A letter was found beside him. Yesterday morning, the Criminal Section of the French Police summoned the deceased's mother, Jiang, and aunt, Wen Shen, to the station and reported to Judge Zhu of the French Public Concession to examine the body. He sat in court, and the Bao Detective reported the situation. After Judge Zhu questioned the family of the deceased, he declared that the deceased Wen Linsen had committed suicide by taking poison before his death, and the deceased's mother, Yao Jiang, was allowed to prepare a coffin for burial herself. The suicide note is recorded below: Uncle, Aunt, Parents, Your nephew last told you about everything at home when I went to the Shen's house. Everything that mother said at my aunt's house after you came was completely untrue. I also came out to ask, asking my brother and sister for the money for food from childhood to adulthood. If I don't go out, mother will beat me and scold me to go out, scolding me day and night. The day before yesterday at eleven or twelve o'clock at night, mother was doing improper things outside the back door with someone and was seen by a bystander, who later told me. I also had no way to think. The day before yesterday, my aunt called me to go home, and I let him say. My aunt said to me that he had improper words. He said I would say. If I go home like this, mother said that my aunt sent him to promise to be fully responsible for everything in the family. He said that everything in the shop, including food and clothing, would be included, regardless of whether there was food or not. He asked me to clear up all the money owed in the shop before. Later, when Jiwen's daughter grew up, he would hire another man to take charge, and my brother and sister would give way, and he wouldn't care whether it was good or bad. I think it's not good now. My aunt called me to promise, but I don't want to. I think it's better for me to go to the road to hell if this continues every day. But please don't be sad. If there is a way to avenge me, let him go if there is no way. There is still my younger sister, you must be extra careful. Always look at the face of death and say it for me. I am now waiting at your house and it is difficult to explain. Please forgive me. I am now going to the road to hell to see you all. I can't write anymore, my heart hurts, I can't do it anymore. I'm gone, your nephew Linsen. The above is the general situation.

Notice to Buyers of Used Vehicles 178

▲ Municipal Bureau of Public Works: Yesterday's Announcement

The Municipal Bureau of Public Works issued an announcement yesterday stating: "Regarding the matter of announcements, according to the regulations governing vehicle licenses in this city, when a vehicle is taken out of service, the license plate should be returned to this bureau. Otherwise, the owner remains responsible for paying the fees. However, many vehicle owners neither return the license plates nor pay the fees on time. They then sell the vehicles to others, who reapply for licenses. The bureau regards the vehicle as the primary subject. It can only order the new owners to pay the back fees, which they are unwilling to do, as they are being held responsible for someone else's debt. Yet, the bureau must enforce the regulations and cannot make exceptions. To avoid such disputes, the following two points are announced for the attention of all buyers of used vehicles: (1) Buyers of used automobiles and other motorized vehicles should first submit the license plate and engine numbers to the General Vehicle Affairs Office of this bureau to inquire whether any fees are owed or other violations remain unresolved. (2) Buyers of used horse carriages, rickshaws, and large and small freight vehicles should check whether they have a steel-stamped number from this bureau. If there is a steel-stamped number, they should immediately inquire at the nearest Vehicle Affairs Office of this bureau whether any fees are owed or other violations remain unresolved."

Commercial Broadcasting Station to Begin Broadcasting Next Spring 179

▲ Chinese United Wireless Electric Company Manufactures Its Own Equipment

The Chinese United Wireless Electric Company, located at 3 Museum Road, has been dedicated to operating a wireless electric business since its establishment. It manufactures various standard transmitting and receiving machines and broadcasting equipment at low prices and with excellent quality. Therefore, its business is very prosperous. It is currently manufacturing a one-kilowatt broadcasting machine and actively preparing to build a radio station. It is estimated that the station will be completed around the first month of next year. The broadcasting range will focus on commercial information and entertainment, as well as academic lectures and other programs, which will be extremely comprehensive. The company has four manufacturing plants, and the personnel in charge are all domestic wireless electric experts. The scale is large, and the work is precise. The current establishment of a broadcasting station will surely be praised by society. Furthermore, the company also manufactures broadcasting machines of various sizes and power for sale to meet the needs of all sectors wishing to establish broadcasting businesses.

Chinese Corps of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps Wins Distinguished Marksmanship Silver Shield Again 180

▲ Ranked First Among All Seventeen Corps

The Chinese Corps of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps is the most prestigious team in the entire corps. It consistently trains diligently in various subjects and is therefore proficient in marksmanship. Self-discipline has been a characteristic of the corps in the past, and it is even more so now. As a result, in past years, the annual efficiency trophy of the various national teams stationed in Shanghai has often been won by the Chinese Corps. It is now reported that the corps recently received Corps Order No. 110 from the headquarters, announcing that the Chinese Corps has the highest overall score for the year, ranking first among all seventeen corps. The corps will be awarded a Distinguished Marksmanship Silver Shield as an honor. The competition for this shield is extremely strict. To receive the award, one must excel in all aspects of the year's courses, with an average score surpassing all others. The competition courses are divided into five categories: Efficiency, Marksmanship, Drill, Field Operations, Camping, and Defense. In each category, in addition to personal performance, the number of times and people participating in competitions and marksmanship scores must all be excellent to succeed. This year, the Chinese Corps competed with a score of 312.35 points to win first place and subsequently won the most difficult-to-obtain Distinguished Marksmanship Silver Shield in all corps competitions. This is indeed a great achievement. The members of the corps, in addition to expressing their joy together, specially took a group photo to commemorate the event.

Negotiation Over Japanese Ship Crushing Cargo Barge 181

▲ Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Sends Letter Requesting Full Compensation

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, regarding the matter of the Japanese Dalian Steamship Company's ship "Chohei Maru" crushing the cargo barge of the Liyu Oil Firm, sent a letter to the Shanghai Japanese Chamber of Commerce and Industry, forwarding a request for full compensation to the company. The original letter stated: "On the first day of this month, this chamber received a letter from the Chinese Grain, Oil, and Bean Cake Association, a member of this chamber, stating that the Liyu Oil Firm's cargo barge, managed by Mr. He Yinsheng, was loading bean cake at Pier 6 of the Huangpu Wharf on the afternoon of August 26th when it was crushed by the 'Chohei Maru' of the Japanese Dalian Steamship Company. The entire ship capsized, with 800 pieces of bean cake and four containers of bean oil on board. Except for the leakage of the bean oil, all the bean cake sank to the bottom of the Huangpu River, resulting in significant losses. In addition to reporting the incident to the Lujiazui Sub-Bureau of the Water Police and requesting an immediate investigation, we have also requested the River and Sea Customs Tonnage Office to record the incident. We are now writing to your chamber to uphold justice, forward the request to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, negotiate reasonably, and demand compensation to protect commercial interests." The letter included a detailed list of losses. "This chamber has received this communication and especially includes a list of losses. We respectfully request your chamber to consider the difficulties of businesses and provide assistance so that the losses can be compensated." The list of losses was enclosed with the communication. "The cargo barge of the Liyu Oil Firm was crushed by the 'Chohei Maru' of your country's Dalian Steamship Company at Pier 6 of the Huangpu Wharf, causing the entire ship to capsize and resulting in losses to the loaded bean oil cake. According to their estimates, the amount of losses reached 1,495.931 taels of customs silver. This loss to the oil firm should be fully compensated by the Dalian Steamship Company to ensure fairness. Based on the circumstances mentioned in the letter, we are sending the enclosed list to your office, requesting your assistance in forwarding it to the company for investigation and handling. This will truly strengthen our friendship."

Lawyer Da Yaoxian

No Suspicion of Inciting False Testimony 182

▲ Prosecutor Concludes Investigation and Declines to Prosecute

Lawyer Da Yaoxian, while defending Wang Desheng, who was reported by the Mixed Court Police for sending threatening letters, was accused by Wang Yaotang, the lawyer for the police, of attacking the police for using torture to extract confessions. He was accused of inciting Wang Desheng to deny the crime. Wang Desheng's case of being accused of sending threatening letters has already been defended by another lawyer, Ye Fangkang. On July 12th, the Special District Court acquitted Wang Desheng. As for Lawyer Da's part in inciting the retraction of testimony, it has already been submitted to the prosecutor for investigation, as noted in this newspaper. Afterwards, the police believed that since Wang Desheng was acquitted, the report against Lawyer Da should also not be valid. They prepared a letter requesting the court to stop the investigation or allow withdrawal. However, the prosecutor did not approve and continued the investigation according to law. The result was that Lawyer Da Yaoxian was deemed to have been exercising the duties of a lawyer and was not suspected of inciting false testimony. The prosecutor has sent the prepared decision not to prosecute to Lawyer Da for his receipt, and the case is closed.

Coercive Rape Case 183

▲ Conflicting Accounts from Both Parties

The Fourth District Public Security Bureau of Zhabei, yesterday, escorted a case of coercive rape from the Pengpu Township Security Corps, Second Team. Director Jin questioned the plaintiff, Gao Shuxian, a native of Taixing, residing at No. 2 Pingjiang Bridge, Zhonghua Xin Road, earning a living by working. He stated, "My wife, Wang, went out on the afternoon of the first day of this month around 3 PM to visit her younger sisters, hoping to find work in a silk factory. While walking along Pushen Road, she suddenly encountered the defendant, Yang Xiaosanzi, who falsely claimed to be her adoptive mother, calling her to come. My wife believed it to be true and followed him to the home of Chen Yang (i.e., Wang's adoptive mother, the elder sister of Xiaosanzi). Unexpectedly, Xiaosanzi suddenly closed the door. Yang helped drag my wife to the bed, tore off her clothes, and said, 'Don't make a sound. Sleep with me for a day. If you don't agree, I will put a gun to your head and kill you.' My wife was terrified upon hearing this. Fearing his ferocity, she dared not resist and allowed him to ravage her. The next day, she was taken to his own home and confined in a room, not allowed to cross the threshold. She was raped for four consecutive nights. My wife was mentally and physically exhausted and was about to fall ill. Fortunately, she managed to escape the other day and tearfully told me what had happened. I immediately arrested Yang and Chen Yang and reported them to the local Security Corps." According to Gao Wang, 20 years old, "Because of the difficulty of life, I went to ask my younger sisters to introduce me to work. Unexpectedly, Yang Xiaosanzi lured me into his home and threatened and raped me. My adoptive mother actually aided and abetted the abuse. I request a strict investigation." Questioned, Yang Xiaosanzi stated, "I am from Funing, 25 years old, and run a teahouse on Datong Road. I have always been law-abiding. The other day, the plaintiff's wife suddenly came to my place and knocked on my sister's door. I asked her what she wanted. Unexpectedly, she spoke disrespectfully. There was a verbal argument at the time. Unexpectedly, the Security Corps arrested me this morning, saying that I raped Wang. It is completely unjust." Yang stated, 41 years old, "The plaintiff's accusation is completely denied. I am Wang's adoptive mother and Xiaosanzi's sister. How could I do such a shameless thing? Please investigate." Director Jin, noting the conflicting testimonies, ordered that they be sent to the Bureau for interrogation.

Warship and Merchant Ship Collide 188

The Chinese Navy's Weisheng warship was ordered to tow two large iron barges alongside its port and starboard sides to transport goods. Yesterday afternoon at 1 PM, it was traveling from Nanshi toward the lower reaches of the Huangpu River. While passing the outer part of the Swire Group's Huatong Wharf, the Yunnan, a merchant ship fully loaded with cargo and passengers, was moored at the wharf, preparing to depart. At that time, the stern of the ship had already turned outward, and the bow was facing the wharf. The ship was backing up when the Weisheng warship, unable to avoid the sudden appearance of the Yunnan, had the Yunnan's stern violently collide with the iron barge alongside the warship's starboard side. The barge sustained minor damage, while the Yunnan's rudder was damaged and rendered useless, preventing it from traveling. As a result, it temporarily suspended departure, and the cargo and passengers on board had to be refunded or transferred to other ships. The ship returned to the wharf and must be docked for repairs.

Decision Not to Prosecute Local Bully Case 189

▲ Liu Junfu Not Guilty of Soliciting Donations

Liu Junfu, a director of the Huajing Town in Shanghai County, sent vagrant Chen Xinlou to the Caohejing Vagrant Training Center in September of last year. The center released Chen Xinlou because he had a contagious disease. Chen Xinlou complained that Liu Junfu had solicited donations of 100 and 500 yuan. The Shanghai County Government arrested and sent Liu to the local court. Prosecutor Liu Pingfan questioned Liu Junfu, who firmly denied that he had solicited donations. The Vagrant Training Center had donation regulations specifying 500 or 100 yuan. Even if Liu Junfu had actually advised donating, it would not constitute any crime. Therefore, in accordance with Article 244, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Procedure Law, he was given a decision not to prosecute.

Drug Dealers Sentenced to One Year Each 197

▲ Fines of 300 Dollars Each

The other day, drug dealers transporting opium at a wharf on Broadway Road, Hongkou, hired cars for transportation. They were apprehended by the police and arrested and prosecuted in the Special District Court. It has been reported. Yesterday afternoon around 3 PM, a car from the Lanji Auto Company in the French Concession, driven by drivers Zhang Rongyao and Chen A'gen, stopped at the ship wharf at Broadway Road, Yalu Road. A man wearing a blue cloth short shirt and pants jumped out of the car, directing the transfer of four huge paper-wrapped packages into the car. He sped away. Detectives and Detective Feng Qi from the Hua Patrol team became suspicious, believing that they were smuggling contraband. They shouted for them to stop for inspection. The men ignored the orders. The detectives, fearing that they would escape, drew their guns and fired a shot. Their car finally stopped. The man in the blue cloth shirt and pants jumped out of the car and fled. The detectives were unable to catch him. They opened the packages and found them to be full of opium, weighing a total of 1,200 ounces. They arrested the two drivers and took them to the Hongkou station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Special District Court. Judge Feng Shide interrogated them. Police attorney Gan Jingxian said that the two drivers were colluding with the drug dealers and should be severely punished. Chinese and Western detectives reported the circumstances of the investigation. Zhang and others stated that the car was rented by the man in the blue cloth shirt and pants, who said he was picking up guests at the wharf on Broadway Road. They claimed that they did not know that they were transporting drugs. Judge Feng ruled, based on the evidence, that Zhang and Chen should each be sentenced to one year in prison and fined 300 dollars. The opium was confiscated.

Liu Shulun Reports on Banditry in Suqian 202

▲ The Tragic State of Burning, Looting, Killing, and Wounding

The Jiangsu Provisional Relief Committee, at its 37th regular meeting on the 1st of this month, after hearing reports, received a telegram from Liu Shulun, the head of the committee's Suqian Relief Affairs, reporting on the banditry and flood situation in the county. The telegram stated: For several months, Suqian has been plagued by bandits. Since the beginning of summer, continuous rain has made the areas around Yanghe Bu and Gengche, ranging from several to nearly a hundred *li*, affected by disaster. Coupled with the bandits' trampling of farmers' homes, residents are trapped, gazing from their watchtowers. Fields are barren. On the 19th, Shulun went to Bu Zi Ji to distribute relief funds, passing through the west of the old Yellow River embankment, seeing a vast expanse of water and thorns, unable to distinguish crops. When distributing funds, he saw men, women, old, and young, all holding long poles, their faces dark, looking frightened. It was a pitiful sight. The situation is still like this now. How unbearable will it be as the year draws to a close? Other disaster-stricken areas are sending numerous people to the bureau to request investigation and rescue. Although he has politely declined out of necessity, how should he handle this situation? He investigated that in the fourth and fifth districts, apart from those who have already received aid, there are still over two hundred households. While he was in the process of providing supplementary aid, he suddenly heard on the 24th that bandits attacked Caiji and Yangji, burning and killing for over twenty *li*. Refugees fleeing to the city filled the roads, lacking food and shelter, a pitiful sight. He organized two temporary shelters to provide emergency relief. This morning (the 26th), County Magistrate Liu led a team to suppress the bandits. Shulun also accompanied relief friends to conduct an on-site investigation. They found over thirty villages and six hundred households burned, over ten people killed (excluding those looted), and over twenty people wounded. He is currently investigating and providing emergency relief and treating the wounded, etc.

Dispute between Hulink Company and American Silk Merchants 203

▲ Commodity Inspection Bureau's Reply

Shanghai Museum Road No. 15, Hulink Company, engaged in foreign trade, with an agent in the United States to handle a portion of raw silk, recently sold one hundred *dan* of raw silk to the American merchant Scott in April of this year, with a signed contract and inspection certificate. However, the American merchant suddenly refused to acknowledge the contract and threatened to cancel other contracts. The company's manager, Wang Zhusu, petitioned the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting assistance to resolve the issue and avoid losses. The ministry ordered the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau to cooperate with the Industry and Commerce Investigation Bureau to investigate the facts of the original case in detail and report back quickly for verification. Upon receiving the order, the bureau immediately cooperated with Zhang Pansun and Wang Jingxiu of the Industry and Commerce Investigation Bureau and went to Hulink Company for detailed investigation. Shao Yuanxi, director of the company's foreign business department, explained the details of the matter and reviewed all the documents in the case, which were found to be completely consistent with the report to the ministry. The detailed investigation, along with copies of the contract signed by both parties and other documents, has been submitted to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for review.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin would be cloudy with slight thunderstorms, and other areas would have fog. There would be easterly winds over the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. There is a low-pressure system along the coast of Northern Luzon. The hurricane in the Pacific Ocean will continue to move northwest. The highest temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday was 83.5 degrees, and the lowest was 73.6 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 84.6 degrees, and the lowest was 62.0 degrees.

Letter to the Editor 211

To the Esteemed Editor:

In today's edition of your newspaper, on page 4, section 14, in the local news column, the item about the posthumous honors for Yuan Guanlan stated, "According to news from the Yuan residence, the funeral will be held on the 11th of this month." This is a rumor and an error. The date for the funeral has not yet been determined. However, the family's coffin will be temporarily moved to the Shanghai Nanshi Yongxi Chang Shaoxing Guild Hall on the 12th. Because we did not want to trouble relatives and friends, we did not send out notices. Please correct this. We would be most grateful.

Respectfully,

The Yuan Residence

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Buried Beneath Ancient Remains 214

— Gao Wei

By Ying Ang

It seems that young people in general, when faced with the traces of past lives, invariably harbor disappointment or sorrow. Their hope is simply that the past be considered dead and buried at the gate of eternal life. Although they inevitably recall it endlessly, they feel the void filled by the imperfections experienced in the past, and plan for future changes. Now, young people’s attitude towards literature and art seems to be the same. Most young people cannot escape the oppression and constraints of the real environment. To comfort the hardships of these struggles and to imprint them, the only path worth pursuing is literature and art. Only through the expression of literary and artistic forms can one comfort and make up for that certain part of the defect. This is not a so-called opportunistic method. In such an era, only the nourishment of literature and art can satisfy the upward-striving will of young people's ideals. Besides this path, it can almost be said that there is no second path that can supply them, allowing them to immediately regain their original vitality after a period of fatigue and move towards the bright road ahead. This may not be a bad phenomenon.

However, some works by young people are certainly honest, but they often form the knot of the Chinese nation because of temporary complaints or momentary enthusiasm. Young people are naturally restless, and there are not a few who piece things together into articles. When I saw the table of contents of Mr. Ying Ang's book "Buried Beneath Ancient Remains," I suspected that the author's book might also have fallen into the morbid state I mentioned above, because the light sketch on the cover unintentionally symbolized it. Indeed, not unexpectedly, I found the author's own confession in the (Small Preface). He said, "Perhaps those images will never remain. If I didn't have a pen at the time, the materials that are now being thrown into the furnace would not be these. Even if some did come, they might not have been cast so clumsily. So, what is buried here are ancient remains." His attitude was simply that "once upon a time, I was moved to write, and unknowingly left traces of words. The traces of words unexpectedly pieced together into sentences. In some sentences, I couldn't help but reflect on the outlines of several stories." It is difficult to achieve good results writing novels with this attitude. I hope the author will strive to overcome it in the future.

This contains five short stories: ("Mr. Shi and His Story"), ("A Foreigner in China"), ("From Dusk to Twilight"), ("The Rise and Fall of Characters in Temple Lane"), and ("The Completion of Taste"). Among these, the depiction of Mr. Shi's story is the best.

("Mr. Shi and His Story") is about an interesting character. He is a local gentleman, a Chinese language teacher in a foreign school, and a correspondent for a Shanghai newspaper. Thus, Mr. Shi occupies a seemingly significant position in the local society, academic circles, and press. Relying on the power of the foreign school, he can ignore whether the news offends people, because in the midst of chaos, he can squat in the foreign school for a while and not go out. After a few days of leisure, everything will be fine. But the matter is really strange. The government suddenly arrested Mr. Shi, causing local people to rush to send telegrams to rescue him. As a result, this arrest turned into a gain for Mr. Shi. ("Perhaps this is a trick of both sides. The government had no choice but to arrest Mr. Shi and then use this release as a means of entanglement. Mr. Shi is a property clearance committee member, and the government suffers no loss, but the sufferers get many benefits.")

Mr. Shi is very aware of current affairs. Soon after the property clearance committee was established, disputes arose. The disputes arose because the committee members snatched Mr. Shi's business. But Mr. Shi is also open-minded. He thinks that there are still many places where he can make up for the loss and have plenty left over, so why bother with this. Secondly, his mind is not only not old-fashioned, but also very new. Although he is also a scholar, he approves of co-education and even threw inkstones at those antiques during meetings. He can speak "Yang Jingbang" dialect and calls his wife "a Miss Tian Tian in the past." He understands the students' tastes and knows their psychology ("Be as sloppy as you can"), but don't provoke his old gentleman's displeasure. In addition, Mr. Shi's experience as a reporter is also very thoughtful. Since learning the lesson of being arrested, the news released by Mr. Shi not only does not offend his superiors, but sometimes includes a few words of flattery, thus benefiting both sides. Why not do it? Moreover, thanks to his connection with the church, Mr. Shi has been able to remarry three times. So, in a word, Mr. Shi is smart.

However, the tide of revolution finally succeeded. In a sudden and drastic change, with the fluttering of the revolutionary army's flags, Mr. Shi also became one of the "Four King Kongs, Eighteen Arhats," and "Thirteen Taibaos, Five Little Ghosts" to be reformed in the local area. Fortunately, Mr. Shi escaped quickly at the time, so he was not reformed out of his life.

After about two hundred days of Mr. Shi's escape, he was still able to return to his hometown. However, it is said that he is no longer teaching or working as a reporter. The title of gentleman has been reformed away. It is thought that Mr. Shi is not doing that, but I wonder when Mr. Shi will be able to get another committee position to do. This is much more fashionable than before. (Page 28)

Then Mr. Shi will eventually have a day to regain his strength.

People like Mr. Shi, with minor differences, as far as I have seen personally, can be replaced by numbers. Especially in the situation of my hometown, in this sudden change of revolution, if I were to find characters similar to Mr. Shi, it would be a very easy thing. Sometimes, in the extreme of anger, I have tried my best to earnestly find these people, melt them into creation, and leave a trace for them, while promoting general reflection. But it has not been completed, which is truly regrettable. Now that I have read this article, it can be regarded as expressing the accumulation in my heart.

I also like ("The Completion of Taste") very much. It describes the psychology of a man with a wife who has not been well cared for, who wants to make life a little more comfortable and be able to work in peace, so he thinks of taking a concubine. The feeling is very powerful. Originally, in the whole book, the author's psychological descriptions are not many, and mostly only use actions to reflect the characters' psychological states, but here it turns to a deep psychological description.

(Entering the gate of spring, seeing the glittering and restless dark clouds, the hope before the dark clouds is that someone must be brought in to be a concubine. This is the crystallization of a lifetime of brewing. In my heart, I wish that the dark clouds are an unchangeable crystal product that can accompany me throughout my life.) (Page 110)

This completely exposes a person who is eagerly looking forward to the pursuit of happiness.

Page 26

Secondly, I also like the old man in ("From Dusk to Twilight") very much. However, this old man is too purely Eastern. He only knows how to live plainly, from birth to death, without the "will to progress" and "desire to create." In this modern era where we want to express the spirit of our nation, it seems that such characters do not need to be expressed, because for us, living is not just living, but should be rich in the will to live, so that the life of the nation can be strong. If our lives are just mechanical and lifeless, what is the point?

Because the author uses the attitude of "piecing together sentences with traces of words" to write, each article has a kind of hasty state, that is, although the text is finished, there are still many things in the epilogue worth remembering. The author does not continue to write, so the structure cannot be complete, and there is also a suspicion of uneven writing. If he could write with an honest attitude, I don't think there would be such a result.

Founding Issue of Changfeng Monthly 215

— Tang Bin

The fact has already clearly announced to us that advocating nationalistic literature and art is a matter that cannot be delayed at present. In the so-called "loose sand" of China, only this kind of literature and art that conforms to the trend of the times is the path for future research on literature and art, because it has a long historical background. Everyone knows that China has a culture that is five thousand years ahead of the world, and in the past, it made many contributions to the academic circles of the world. Even the earliest and most reliable collection of poetry, the Book of Songs, was aware of extremely profound nationalistic thought at that time. This is generally recognized by scholars. Therefore, advocating nationalistic literature and art in the current China, where the ideological circles are chaotic and decadent, has a very broad significance. Everyone should joyfully and enthusiastically sing its rise. Therefore, since the publication of the most powerful (Avant-Garde Weekly) in promoting nationalistic literature and art, the literary world in the country has been greatly revitalized. There is a rapid development in academic progress and the rise of publications. Taking Shanghai, the cultural center, as an example, there have been many that have risen or have had an impact on them, such as (Era Youth), which guides students in logical reasoning, and (Caoye Weekly), which focuses on creative news and is quick. All of these take nationalism as the center of their efforts in literature and art. In other places, there are also many publications about this kind of literature and art being produced, especially in our capital, which has a new atmosphere. This shines with infinitely bright and brilliant hope for the future of China's academic circles, which are becoming increasingly backward. The revival of Chinese culture, shining a unique light on the world's literary scene, can be predicted with certainty that this will happen in the near future.

The (Changfeng Monthly) that I am now going to introduce to readers who love literature and art is one of the publications that has recently appeared in the publishing world of the capital.

In the Chinese publishing world, where ideological confusion is unbearable, many scholars who specialize in literature and art urgently need to clean it up. It is really not right to allow it to remain chaotic for a long time. Therefore, the large and small publications currently published all grasp a consistent central idea in essence, and very clearly and thoroughly promote to readers what they advocate and believe in, and draw a clear line of their own battle lines. This is the initial step to clear up the unbearable ideological confusion. Therefore, this Changfeng Monthly, which takes "introducing world scholarship and promoting national spirit as its purpose," also takes on its mission in literature and art, and clearly expresses itself to us at the beginning. At the same time, it also discusses politics, but culture and politics have a close connection and cannot be separated. This is a fact.

The cultural history of mankind for thousands of years is the product of thought. The new inventions and new sciences of the twentieth century are also all products of thought. The division between humans and other animals is that the former has a larger scope of intellectual activity, while the latter has a smaller scope of intellectual activity. The rise and fall of nations, the superiority and inferiority of culture, and the excellence or inferiority of politics are all determined by people's thoughts. Hegel (Heael) said, "The authority of thought is fiercer than the raging fire of hell." Is that a lie?

These are indeed sharp words. Originally, "animals have intelligence, but not as great as human intelligence." If we want the country to be strong, we must start by working hard on the national literature of the country to which we belong. Therefore, promoting the national literature and art movement cannot be delayed any longer, because we really need to know the two great missions that this (Changfeng Monthly) sincerely undertakes.

We have seen the unbearable confusion and decadence of the Chinese ideological circles, and we also know that only from the academic standpoint can we sort out the confused and decadent thoughts. Therefore, we have to devote ourselves to the movement of sorting out thoughts. The motive for publishing this publication is conceived here. This publication has two major missions: one is to introduce world scholarship, and the other is to promote national spirit. China is not only backward in industry, but also in scholarship. The danger of academic famine is greater than the danger of material famine. If others' scholarship advances rapidly, and we do not catch up, we will not only always fall behind, but we will also not be able to survive, because the competition for survival is becoming increasingly fierce. The weapon of competition is scholarship. Those with scholarship live, those without scholarship die. Those whose scholarship progresses win, those whose scholarship is naive lose. Why can't we resist the imperialist aggression in China for eighty years, and let them slaughter us? Isn't it because their scholarship is stronger than ours? Otherwise, since we are all human beings, why do they have organization, planning, and can use scientific methods in everything, while we cannot? If the Chinese do not work hard to become strong, if we want to get rid of the mark of a semi-colony and wash away the great shame of the past eighty years, there is no other way but to strive for academic development.

We are the Chinese nation, and of course we should not forget Chinese culture, let alone sit idly by and watch Chinese culture fall into a state of never reviving. At the same time, we must sacrifice some precious brainpower and find out the cause and effect of why Chinese culture, despite having more than 5,000 years of history, cannot leap to the forefront of the world. Regarding this, the paragraph quoted above explains it to us thoroughly and without omission. It also seems like needle pricks, and every word touches the hearts of Chinese scholars and young people who love literature and art, arousing the heart to strive hard to promote Chinese national literature. But we must know that we have now reached an era of (hanging by a thread). It is like a blazing torch burning behind us, and the people in front have to bravely rise up their spirits and rush forward. Do you still hesitate to move forward? Then, you will not only not be able to stand still, but you will also be in danger of losing your life.

Secondly, the publication has a more detailed explanation of the two missions it undertakes. Due to the limitations of the publication's space, we can only abandon the introduction of world scholarship, and only quote the second mission it wants to accomplish. But the points it discusses are very precise and thorough. For those of us who love literature and art, we have no choice but to read it with pleasure, because it has many places that can be used as a reference for those who strive for national literature and art. I hope readers will read it with a calm mind. It is developing so powerfully:

The second mission of this publication is to promote the national spirit. Nationalism is certainly not enough to be a lesson, but the national spirit must be promoted with all our strength. Everyone knows that the nation is different from the country, and there is no need to explain it. The Chinese nation has shown a special brilliance in history. The contribution of the Chinese nation to human culture has been recognized by scholars all over the world. However, since the Opium War, the Chinese nation has gradually fallen into the position of a semi-colony, and there is a tendency to be in danger of perishing from morning till evening. Why is it so weak? There are at least half a dozen reasons for its weakness, but the biggest reason is the loss of national spirit. This point is explained in detail by the President in the Three Principles of the People. The national spirit is the marrow of the national culture. If the national spirit cannot be promoted, the national culture will inevitably wither. ... Gandhi's sacrifice for the Indian nation, Kemal's contribution to the Turkish nation, and the independence movements of the Korean, Annamese, Filipino, and Persian nations are all manifestations of the development of national consciousness. This kind of movement is the cry of various nations for freedom and equality, and it is the expression of all mankind seeking light and realizing justice. If things are not fair, they will cry out. If the gap between the oppressed and the oppressors cannot be bridged between nations, mankind will never have a day of security. It can be seen that the efforts of various nations to seek solutions are indeed self-help and helping others, because the spirit of nationalism and the spirit of internationalism are originally the same. Nationalism is the foundation of internationalism. Only nationalism is the enemy of internationalism. Therefore, promoting the national spirit is not only a means for a nation to liberate itself, but also a harbinger of the great unity of mankind.

We have a clear understanding of the purpose of the publication and the tasks that should be completed. Now, we need to examine its contents. However, the unity of thought and grasping the central consciousness of the nation is inevitable and does not need to be repeated. It is divided into (Special Discussion) and (Literature and Art) columns. The former contains six great works, and the latter contains eight chapters of poetry, scholarship, and novels. Equal emphasis is placed on translation and creation, which is in line with the two great missions that the publication undertakes. In the (Special Discussion) column, there are also discussions about science, education, and youth issues. These are all precise and great works, which greatly benefit our readers. Finally, there are three miscellaneous essays attached, which also have a rather sharp flavor.

Violin Virtuoso Chen Dunlis to Perform in Shanghai 216

Chen Dunlis (Zimbalist), a famous modern violinist, is highly praised in Europe and the United States. Recently, he has been touring the Far East to perform. Mr. Chen arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and is scheduled to perform once tonight (Sunday) at the Xia Ling Pei Ying. The program is all world-famous classical and modern pieces. The time is set to be from 9:15 p.m. The ticket prices are divided into two types: five yuan and two and a half yuan.

Group News 217

▲ The Minzhi Popular Propaganda Group declared that the group held a supplementary election meeting at 8:00 p.m. on the 4th day before yesterday at Sanwei Lane, Manzhou Road, Zhabei. About twenty or thirty members attended. Wang Xingquan was publicly elected as chairman and Lu Zhiqian as recorder. The ceremony was held as usual. The chairman reported on the problems of the quorum being lacking and the need for today's meeting. Next, Li Yongxiang, representative of the Municipal Party Department, Gu Zenghong, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, and Wen Ren'an, representative of the Sixth District Party Department, gave speeches in succession (length omitted). Then, the articles of association were discussed and revised. Afterwards, in accordance with the articles of association, seven people were organized and elected to fill the positions of alternate executive committee members and supervisors. Zhou Junying, Cai Fuyu, and Zhang Chunsheng were elected as alternate executive committee members at that time. Gong Yunding, Bu Chang, and Liang Yuling were elected as supervisors. Qian Shuntao was elected as an alternate supervisor. The group is scheduled to hold a formal swearing-in ceremony this afternoon.

▲ The Alumni Association of the Sino-French School declared that the association has been established for more than five years and has achieved remarkable results. Recently, in order to develop the association's affairs, an annual meeting will be held today at the Pacific Western Restaurant on Avenue Edward VII, and the progress will be reported. Alumni are welcome to participate enthusiastically. The association has already published a monthly magazine with rich content, including discussions, artistic photographs, cartoons, novels, meeting minutes, and accounting reports. One issue is published every month and three issues have already been published. It is a non-selling item and will be sent upon request by letter.

Theater News 218

▲ Baixing Grand Theater declared that since its renovation, the Fuxing Road Baixing Grand Theater has been carefully selecting films. Now it is opening the world's most talented and versatile portrayal of the romantic master John Barrymore starring in The Tempest, a giant film about the war between the Red and White parties in Russia.

▲ New Allen Grand Theater declared that the theater is holding its fourth anniversary celebration and is offering half-price tickets, and has selected The Wilderness Woman Knight produced by the Youlian Company to promote it widely.

▲ Guanghua Grand Theater on Avenue Edward VII declared that the theater has recently opened the film The Devil Comes to Earth, which is always full. A famous music team has also been invited to help boost the excitement.

▲ Guomin Grand Theater on Zha Pu Road declared that the theater will open The Tiger's Den Beauty Snatch, starring Raymondo De Rolo, today, which is a world-famous giant film about naval battles.

▲ Yueming Film Company declared that in the second episode of The Female镖師, which was recently filmed, the scene of a giant python biting a person was filmed at the studio yesterday. The python was more than two zhang long and had eyes like electric torches, which made people afraid to look at it. Director Peng Nian used it as a poisonous object used by local tyrants to harm people. The danger made people gasp. On the same day, the flying axe mechanism was also filmed. The protagonist of the play, Hercules Cha Rui Long, jumped down from the top of a house more than ten zhang high and passed through it. Jie Li Yun played Qin Hui Zhu in the play, and her performance was very accurate in her act of saving Cha out of righteousness. Wu Lizhu, dressed as a man, also showed her heroic qualities and showed off her skills in flying over walls. The interior scenes of the third episode of The Female镖師 have already been filmed for the most part. The two new films, The Great Heroes of Guandong in the seventh and eighth episodes, are also actively underway and will be filmed soon.

Publishing News 219

▲ Shanghai Caoye Society, No. 34, Feilun Road, declared that the third volume, issue 6 of the Caoye Weekly published by the society was originally scheduled to be published, but it was postponed due to damage to the printing press's machinery. Later, it could not be published because the main leader, Mr. Jin Kuansheng, was slightly ill for ten days and lacked assistants. As a result, the third volume, issue 7, which should have been published yesterday, has not been published either. Now Mr. Jin Kuansheng has recovered from his illness, and the replies from the society's friends have also been sent out one after another. The Caoye manuscripts have been sorted through once and are being rushed to press. It is expected to be published as usual on the 13th of this month. At the same time, the third volume, issues 6 and 7 will be published as supplements. Many readers have sent letters to inquire. In addition to answering them one by one, this is a special announcement. Please forgive me.

▲ Youth Friends Society declared that the Youth Friends Weekly, since its publication, has been praised by aspiring young people because it can move forward continuously and meet the needs of the times. The number of copies sold has been increasing daily. The 58th issue has been published today. The content is richer than before. Major bookstores in this city, such as Beixin, Xinyue, and Qingyun, as well as newspaper vendors, are all acting as agents for sales.

Medical News 220

▲Mr. Zhao Bingsheng, the French translator for the French Concession's Big Ben Fire Brigade, suddenly suffered from blood poisoning a month ago. He suddenly felt pain in his limbs, had difficulty walking, and was absent from his duties for more than a month. He suffered both mentally and physically. Fortunately, he was introduced by a friend to Dr. Shen Yunfei of Gui Xin Li, South Chengdu Road, who diagnosed and treated him with injections. Within a few days, he recovered completely. Mr. Zhao and his entire family were endlessly grateful.

▲The German Huada Pharmacy at 259 Foch Road declares that the Lion Brand Beef Juice from the German Martha Pharmaceutical Factory, which is managed by the pharmacy, has been very popular among the elite since it was sold in China. This beef juice is effective in increasing energy and strengthening the body, nourishing the brain and strengthening the blood, and can also nourish the stomach and prevent dysentery. It is an unparalleled treasure for patients and those with weak constitutions. Due to the high demand, it was out of stock for three weeks, but more than two thousand boxes have already arrived. It is sold in major companies, pharmacies, food stores, and dry goods stores in this city.

Shen Bao Pictorial Weekly

(1) The British airship R-100 departed from Cardington on July 29th and arrived safely at St. Hubert Station in Montreal, Canada on August 1st. The long journey of more than 3,000 miles took only 78 hours and 51 minutes.

The composition of the so-called (British Empire) relies entirely on transportation. In the past, warships were practical tools for national defense equipment and liaison, but now aircraft are also used and promoted without reservation. Last year, the British had already established two major air routes between London, Berlin, Moscow, and London, Cairo, and Karachi. This year, Ms. Gong Sheng broke the previous record for long-distance flights between England and Australia in three weeks. Recently, the R-100 airship completed the long-distance flight between England and Canada across the Atlantic in 79 hours. This not only opened a new era in transportation, but also strengthened the close relationship between the British Empire and its colonies. The significance of this is something we cannot ignore.

(2) The crew of the British airship R-100 are welcomed in the capital of Canada. The person in gray clothing in the center is Mr. Kong Maomao, the representative of the British Aviation Department. The first person on the right is Captain Booth.

(3) The majestic appearance of the British airship R-101 in the sky above London. This is the sister ship of the R-100 and competes with the German Graf Zeppelin airship.

(4) British aviator Ms. Gong Sheng flew alone from England to Australia in May, exceeding the previous record. She arrived in London on August 4th and was warmly welcomed by local officials and people.

(5) The American aircraft "Datotama," which is preparing to make a trans-Pacific flight from Japan, arrived in Kasuga after being assembled. At the time, Lieutenant Brownell was shaking hands with Japanese Aviation Commander Kobayashi.

(6) In order to enable young people to understand the structure of airplanes, the importance of the aviation industry, and its relationship to national defense, the Japanese have opened schools and aviation associations at the Tachikawa Airfield in Tokyo.

(7) Riots broke out in Cairo, Egypt on July 21, resulting in one death and 87 injuries. The reason was that the National Party accused the current cabinet of oppressing democracy and demanded that the King of Egypt abdicate. This is a scene of clashes between the masses and the military police.

(8) American economist Professor Gong Sheng asked Mrs. Lenin about the truth of the emergence of the Soviet Russian government in order to engage in writing.
